Chamber of Commerce Eulogy 76

On December 11th of the 21st year of the Republic of China, Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and Ye Chunnian, Head of the 50th Troop of the Boy Scouts of China, and Deputy Head Xu Guozhi, led all the members to offer sacrifices to the spirits of the four martyrs Luo Bao Ying Mao who were martyred in the Songhu War, alas, the dwarf bandits were rampant, the Songhu was polluted, the cannons and fire filled the sky, the gun forest and bullet office, the huts were in ruins, the corpses lay across the suburbs, the Chinese territory, suffered this humiliation, the ambitious youth, how could they be female, because of the red blood and declared the alliance, went to the battlefield and served, Wu Zhi was captured and killed, and died without yielding, the awe-inspiring righteousness, made people admire, turned to the tragic situation, thought of the tears, the youth of the enemy country, Luo This tragic situation, drinking hatred for life, the corpses are nowhere to be found, alas, from this secluded underworld forever separated, no longer a time to talk, the merit of serving the country was not achieved, the great disaster of killing the body was approaching, why did the heavens not mourn, and take my pillar, why did the land not bow, and lose my beam, lamenting that the violent sun has receded, and the Shanghai, is still based in the northeast, clearly opened the puppet, secretly planned the sinister, although we are on the seat of the house, the people of the north are still in a dangerous situation, difficult to settle, what is my happiness, turning over and over, no different from hell, mourning my compatriots, fish and meat, the heroic soul of the martyr, I pray for your assistance, inherit the legacy, the responsibility of the living, respectfully erect a inscription, to record the memory, the towering heroic name, will last forever and bury the clothes and hats, entrust the drifting, the spirit knows, to enjoy and to visit,

Mr. Wang's Speech 77

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Chairman Wang Xiaolai's speech, today the Boy Scouts of our city's Chamber of Commerce, opened a memorial service for the Luo Mao Ying Bao four members who were martyred in the Songhu War, Cheng Party, government, military organs, and all circles came to Bao, and came to pay their respects, one side is to express respect for the dead, and the other side is for the national crisis that continues to come, I want to take this opportunity to arouse deep awareness and seek a great self-help method, so we initiated this meeting, and the meaning of each sector is not to pretend to be a scene, or to join in the fun. Xiaolai, in the name of the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, has a closer relationship, and because I instructed them to serve, so today I have unlimited sadness, first, this Boy Scout is trained by the Chamber of Commerce, their relationship with the Chamber of Commerce is like a father and son. The martyrdom of the four members is like the martyrdom of their own children. These four people are all brave and promising young people. They should do a lot of things when they are alive. In this way, they will be buried, and they will not even see their bodies, which is really a sad thing. But from another perspective, Taishigong said something like this, called death heavier than Mount Tai, and lighter than a feather, so their death, died for saving compatriots, died for not surrendering to the enemy, is the glory of the Chinese Boy Scouts, and the glory of the families of the four members, and the glory of the 400 million people of our Chinese nation, in other words, do our children not want them to be Shi Kefa or Wen Tianxiang, and must they be Zheng Xiaoxu or Yu Chonghan? I think no father will want this. Boy Scouts serving on the battlefield, because he is a rescuer, not a combatant, originally there is no reason for him to be killed by the enemy, but how can they waste these reasons? Now the national crisis is expanding day by day, and the spirit of our Boy Scouts' service must also increase day by day, and the places to sacrifice in the future will not be many. The country has reached this point, we cannot avoid danger, we can only harden our scalp and go to work on the road of self-help, so I hope that our Boy Scouts, and the families of our Boy Scouts, will encourage courage and not be discouraged by the tragic death of the four members. Second, our memorial service is not a joke, but to make the compatriots in the country who have not suffered disasters, turn around and think about it, our Northeast has thousands and thousands of volunteers who are fighting the enemy desperately, those who died died, those who were injured were injured, isn't the tragic and enthusiastic situation hundreds or thousands of times more than our Boy Scouts? Then, who else is holding a memorial service? Why not? Because the people of the East and the two provinces have become the people of a fallen country, if you want to express something, he will treat you as a traitor and kill you happily, as the old saying goes, called death without a burial place, the volunteers in the three northeastern provinces have reached the point of death without a burial place, so today's memorial service is not just a memorial service for our four Boy Scout martyrs, but also a memorial service for the thousands and thousands of unnamed heroes who died to resist Japan, but what is the use of just memorializing? We must have the determination to recover the lost territory, and the preparation to recover the lost territory, then today's memorial service is meaningful, the conditions for Boy Scouts are the three words of wisdom, benevolence, and courage, I say that our work of saving the country cannot be separated from these three words. Confucius explained the definition of wisdom, benevolence, and courage, called good learning is close to wisdom, practicing is close to benevolence, and knowing shame is close to courage. These three sentences are really prescribing medicine according to the current situation. To save the country, we must first study knowledge, and it is impossible without wisdom, to save the country, we must do it in a concrete way, and empty words are not enough, this is the definition of the four words of wisdom and benevolence, the meaning of the third sentence is more profound. The 19th Route Army and the Northeast Volunteer Army, in terms of material equipment, no one can compare with the enemy, the reason why they died as women, is because they deeply imprinted the two words of national shame in their minds, so they are not afraid of anything, this is called knowing shame is close to courage, so our memorial is not to join in the fun, but to ask everyone to take the three words of wisdom, benevolence, and courage as a creed, and take on this responsibility of saving the country together, this is Xiaolai's personal thoughts, if there is anything wrong, please ask the guests to correct me.

Xu's Speech 78

Zhu Jiahua, the Preparatory Director of the Chinese Boy Scouts Association, gave a speech on behalf of Xu Guanyu, saying, "Today's memorial service for the four Boy Scout martyrs is the most sorrowful and glorious gathering in the history of the Chinese Boy Scouts. Why? Because the younger generation is to be held in awe, and the future of young people is limitless. The loss of one young person is a loss to the country. In particular, older people have a warmer feeling for the younger generation, and they feel particularly saddened by this kind of loss. What's more, the sacrifice and suffering of these four Boy Scout martyrs are beyond description in words. Secondly, why do we feel it is the most glorious? We all know that the existence of human life has two elements: one is the physical body, and the other is the spirit. However, the physical body is limited by time. Whether it is humans or chickens and geese, they cannot resist the coming of death. However, the spirit is eternal. We seek the eternity of the spirit even at the cost of sacrificing our lives, and this is our noblest behavior. So, how can we make the spirit last forever? It is to contribute our personality, affairs, scholarship, words, and deeds to human beings, achieve the world, raise the status of the country, and promote the happiness of the nation, just as the ancients said, 'Establish virtue, establish merit, and establish speech.' Now, these four Boy Scout martyrs were brutally murdered because of their love for the country, helping others, serving the community, and assisting refugees. We all know the brutality of the other party's actions, and there is no need to go into details now. But these four martyrs promoted the virtues of the Boy Scouts, sacrificed themselves to save others, and achieved such glory today. Not only will the dead smile in the afterlife, but we, as members of the Chinese Boy Scouts, should all be deeply proud of it. From the above two meanings, we can see that there are two tasks that we need to work hard on in the future. First, we need to think about how to eliminate the grief of today. In other words, we need to think about how to eliminate all the obstacles that cause the grief of the Chinese nation. In simple terms, we need to find a way to seek the independence and freedom of the country and its middle-level international status, so that such grief will not happen again in the future. In recent decades, the deaths of Chinese soldiers and civilians like these four Boy Scouts have not been statistically recorded. If we look at history and recent records, we will know in detail. We must always be vigilant. Second, we must maintain this glory and promote it. How? We can earnestly implement the Boy Scout's oath and regulations, practice the teachings of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen, be a loyal citizen in the country, a good citizen who helps the weak and serves the society in the community, and strive to be a member of the family who shares the responsibilities of parents. That's all. If every Boy Scout is like this, and every Chinese youth is like this, the Chinese nation will naturally become great and strong and will no longer be insulted or bullied. Since this is the case, how should we strive to realize the above two tasks? We should not be discouraged, abandon ourselves, or be sad in the future. Only if everyone is willing to hold their heads high and chest out, be as hardworking and responsible as a camel, as great and brave as a lion, as lively and alert as a hunting dog, and as gentle and peaceful as a sheep, and recognize that the blood shed by the martyrs is illuminating the path for us

Page 11

to build a new China of the people, by the people, and for the people. Then, one day, we will reach the goal we hope for. The late Premier taught us, 'Peace, struggle, and save China.' Let's encourage each other."

Erecting a Monument 79

The monument to the four martyrs was built in front of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's auditorium, facing northeast. It was constructed by the Xin Jin Ji Construction Company at a semi-voluntary cost of over 700 yuan. It is about two zhang tall and one zhang square, surrounded by iron railings and adorned with gold lettering. The top of the spire and iron fence is crowned with the Boy Scout emblem, and the surrounding area is densely planted with flowers, grass, and trees, creating a very solemn atmosphere. Cai Tingkai, the army commander of the 19th Route Army, inscribed the four large characters "Sacrifice for the Country." The inscription on the monument was written by Wang Xiaolai, the chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce: "On January 28, 1932, the Japanese army attacked Zhabei and failed, and then the army, navy, and air force attacked Shanghai in separate routes. In order to rescue refugees and wounded soldiers, this chamber dispatched Boy Scouts to form rescue teams for rescue and care. Members Wei Yunxiang, Mao Zhengxiang, Ying Wenda, and Bao Zhengwu, four non-combatants, were killed by the enemy. This is unheard of in international law. We have collected funds to comfort their families, and erected a monument next to the courtyard of this chamber to record the circumstances of the four men's martyrdom, in order to express their loyalty and inspire future generations. Alas, the souls of the pioneers have not returned, and the barbarians are already grazing their horses in the south. Let those who come after us strive for the cause. This inscription was written on the anniversary of the national crisis on September 18, 1932."

Holding an Unveiling Ceremony 80

After the memorial service, a ceremony was held to unveil the monument. Representatives from all walks of life stood in front of the monument. After the music was played, Chairman Wang Xiaolai delivered a speech, saying, "Today, we are holding the unveiling ceremony of the monument. We must permanently commemorate the martyrdom of the four martyrs. The spirit of the four martyrs will never die and will last forever. Long live the Chinese Boy Scouts!" Then, the national flag covering the monument was unveiled, and flowers were offered. Finally, music was played, and the ceremony ended. It was already past 5 o'clock.

Central Committee Members Staying in Shanghai Held a Discussion Meeting Yesterday 81

Discussing Proposals and Exchanging Meeting Opinions

The Third Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee will be held in Nanjing on the 15th. Central Committee members staying in Shanghai, except for Yu Youren, Wang Luyi, and Wu Tiecheng, who had already left for Nanjing last night, the remaining Central Committee members will leave for Nanjing in the next two days. The Central Committee members in Shanghai held a discussion meeting last night to exchange proposal opinions. The following is a record of the news:

Yesterday's Meeting 82

Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, Central Committee members held a discussion meeting at 469 Racecourse Road. Sun Zhesheng, Wu Tiyun, Qin Zhen, Ma Chaojun, Zhang Huichang, Zhang Zhiben, Li Liejun, Liang Hancao, Chen Qingyun, Deng Jiayan, Bai Wenwei, Zhang Dingfan, Wang Faqin, Yang Shukan, Jing Hengyi, Cui Guangxiu, Deng Qingyang, Guan Suren, Li Qian, and over twenty other people attended. During the meeting, Sun and others reported on the contents of Sun's proposals. Zhang Zhiben and Bai Wenwei reported on their experiences in Hong Kong and Guangdong. Guangdong Committee member Guan Suren and others also reported on the opinions of various committees in Guangdong. The committees exchanged opinions, and the meeting adjourned at 5:30 PM.

Proposals of the Committees 83

According to a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency, Sun Zhesheng's proposals are of two types. One focuses on diplomacy, namely, "Concentrate National Strength to Save the Crisis," and its content is based on the previous national salvation program with slight modifications. The other concerns the reform of the party and government, namely, "Reorganize the Party and Government and Implement Policies." In addition, most of the other committees' proposals concern the suppression of bandits and the opinions of the Lytton Report. Sun's proposals have the names of many people listed on them.

Yu Youren Talks About the Opinions of the Third Plenary Session 84

Going to Nanjing with Wang Luyi and others Last Night

Central Committee member Yu Youren left for Nanjing by night train at 11:00 PM last night. Central Committee member Wang Luyi and Liu Kaizhong, the Secretary-General of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, also went to Nanjing with him. Before leaving, Yu told reporters that he was going to Nanjing to attend the Third Plenary Session. The important significance of this plenary session is to review the resolutions of the First and Second Plenary Sessions, to ensure that they are implemented, and to enable all parties to unite sincerely and share the responsibility of resolving the national crisis and opening the way for the advancement of party affairs and politics. The plenary session must have this spirit and this result. This is not only the unanimous wish of the party, but also the hope of the people of the whole country. Therefore, he hoped that all Central Committee members would attend the meeting to make the spirit of the meeting more substantial. This time, attention is not only paid to the number of people, but also to the gathering of Central Committee members in the capital to discuss matters. As for the proposals, etc., they will have to wait until after arriving in Nanjing and waiting for the Central Committee members to arrive before discussing them.

Central Committee member Wang Luyi and Liu Kaizhong, Secretary-General of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, came to Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning because the Third Plenary Session was imminent. They urged President Wang to return to Nanjing and learned that Minister He Yingqin of the Ministry of Military Affairs was receiving medical treatment in Shanghai. They specifically went to inquire about his condition. It is said that He has recovered his health and will be able to return to Nanjing to attend the meeting soon. Wang and others also visited Bai Liewu and Fu Rulin, Central Committee members, and accompanied President Yu back to Nanjing by night train last night.

He Xiangning Will Not Attend the Third Plenary Session 85

Unwilling to Force Herself to Go to Nanjing

Central Committee member He Xiangning replied yesterday to a letter from the Special Party Department of the 15th Army Division, saying, "Since the September 18th Incident, I returned to China. Not long after, the Shanghai war broke out, and I engaged in relief work. During this time of national crisis, I have fulfilled the responsibility of a citizen, which led to illness and heart disease. I have been bedridden for more than half a year. Following the advice of doctors, I have been resting behind closed doors and have declined worldly affairs. The carriages in front of my door have long since disappeared. Now I have received letters from the Central Committee and your Special Party Department urging me to go to Nanjing to attend the Third Plenary Session. I believe that the national situation has been critical for a long time. There are many respected figures and famous party and state figures who are attending. If everyone can show sincerity and work together to overcome the national crisis, the attendance of one or two people will not be a problem. Otherwise, what good would it do? With my ailing body, lacking strategies for restoring the country and relieving the people, I would be of no help. I am unwilling to force myself to go to Nanjing and worsen my illness. If the pillars of the party and the state can be mindful of the precariousness of the national situation and the suffering of the people, reverse the practices of the past, and vigorously implement the National Revolution of Premier Sun and resist imperialism, restoring the revolutionary spirit of the Thirteenth Year of the Republic, then even if I die ten thousand times, I would not dare refuse, let alone cherish my sick body. I ask myself that I have no connection with any political factions. All those who can relieve the suffering of the people and bring glory to the nation are my friends; otherwise, they are my enemies. This is my humble opinion. Whether you understand me or blame me, I do not care. He Xiangning."

Survey of Embankment Works in Bandit Areas 86

Embankment Works in Bandit Areas 87

Going westward from Hankou along the Yangtze River, from Xindi to Jianli, has always been an area where communists have been active. Honghu, their base, is nearby. After a thorough suppression this summer, it was cleared by October. The embankment construction period coincided with the height of communist activity. The embankment works from Xindi to Jianli were under the jurisdiction of the Sixth and Seventh Engineering Bureaus. The work process was extremely difficult. According to Chen Chongwu, director of the Sixth District Labor Relief Bureau, and Chen Zerong, engineer of the Seventh District Labor Relief Bureau, the communist party's brutal killings during the work in the bandit areas were chilling. However, at that time, in order to provide relief to the flood victims and the lives of the people in the area, they resolutely disregarded everything and sent Luo Jingtang, a technician from the first five sections of the Sixth District, and Liu Xianjie, a technician from the last five sections, to the Xindi bandit area to negotiate with the communists about embankment construction methods. At that time, the Soviet Provincial Government of the Xiang and Hubei Provinces under the communist party had established the Xiang-E-West District Riverbank Water Conservancy Committee. After presenting the conditions, it was stipulated that the embankment workers, wages, grain, and the management and control of the workers should be under the full authority of the Soviet government. The Labor Relief Bureau could send supervisors to reside and monitor, and be responsible for contacting the transportation of grain and payment of wages. The Labor Relief Bureau acknowledged and followed these conditions one by one, and then organized the Jianli Embankment Construction Committee, with three members from the Communist Party and two from the Labor Relief Bureau. There was also the Jianli Embankment Construction Supervision Committee, which was entirely filled by communists, so the real power was completely in the hands of the Communist Party. However, because the command was unified and the action was rapid, when construction started, it was planned to recruit 20,000 workers in three days, and it was fully staffed by the second day. In the Guanyin Island area of the Seventh District, because the water flow was turbulent, it was necessary to pump water before the embankment could be built. The communist party organized a women's group to take charge of the water pumping work, and technicians Xue Zuotang and Zhao Guangguo from the Seventh District were appointed as managers, and the order was quite good. After the start of construction, the local security regiment suddenly came to attack. The communists believed that the contact person for the embankment construction had tipped them off, and arrested them, claiming they were spies. After strong arguments and investigations by the communists in all directions, it was proven that the information was inaccurate, and they were able to preserve their lives. At that time, the monthly salary of the communist embankment committee members was only six yuan, the monthly salary of the district government chairman was four yuan, and the wages of the soldiers were eight yuan. It is estimated that among the embankment personnel working in the bandit areas, those who were arrested by the communists included: (1) Four people were arrested in Jiayu, Sixth District, two of whom were released immediately, and the remaining two were detained for more than ten days before being released; (2) Four supervisors and engineers were arrested in Fangjiawan, Ninth District, Xiang River, and released shortly after; (3) Eleven people were arrested in Guanyin Island, Seventh District, at the end of May this year, and were escorted to the Zhuhe bandit government for detention. In August, Zhuhe was recovered, and they regained their freedom, but their hair had grown several inches long and they were no longer recognizable.

Hujia Island New Embankment 88

At 10:00 AM on the 6th, the Wan'an wheel arrived at Hujia Island, about twenty miles from Xindi. The entire delegation disembarked on sampans and walked about a mile to reach the Hujia Island embankment, which was built by the Sixth District Labor Relief Bureau. Beyond this was built by the communists. According to the villagers, there is a security regiment stationed here, so the communists have never been here. Four or five miles from here is Huangmu Mountain, where the communist township government is located. When they were rampant, they would come to harass at night, sometimes a few people, sometimes more than ten, looting property or kidnapping wealthy residents, and the residents could not sleep at night. Those with a little property moved away one after another, and now they are returning one after another. However, the accumulation of years has been completely lost, so hundreds of households in the entire village have become slums. The words are extremely miserable. At that time, the embankment workers lived on the ship, working on the river during the day and returning to the ship to rest at sunset, not daring to stay for a moment. At 11:00 AM, the ship reversed, and the ship drove upstream.

Arriving at Yinji Wharf 89

The Wan'an wheel arrived at Yinji Wharf at 1:00 PM, which is the boundary between Mianyang County and Jianli County, belonging to the Ninth Section Project of the Sixth District. The embankment is the Hongen Embankment, which is ten meters wide and was completely built by the communists. The communists had established the Jianmian Soviet County Government nearby. According to an official from the Sixth District Labor Relief Bureau who was supervising construction here at the time, the communists worked hard because the command was unified. However, the inner and outer slopes of various embankments were not based on engineering principles, but followed the opinions of the villagers. A little resistance would be met with contempt. The communist foremen often made extra demands and harassed endlessly. However, what they got was distributed equally among the workers, without any private corruption. There was a group leader for every four households in the communist party, and the group leader had meetings every day to report on the diligence of work and things when going out and returning. Therefore, there were many eyes and ears, and if any malpractices were discovered, they would be handed over to governments at all levels and punished with the death penalty, without exception. All communists working on the embankment were given passes by the Labor Relief Bureau and could pass through the areas where the army was stationed. As for our supervisors, we lived in a small house next to the district government, with the Red Army guarding outside. When our army attacked, we showed them a specially made blue flag, so they knew we were officials from the Labor Relief Bureau. When the Red Army came, they showed the cloth strips given by the communist side, and they could also enter and exit freely. Therefore, the personnel of the Labor Relief Bureau seemed to be in a third-party position. However, at that time, living in the bandit areas, there were often shameless women ordered to seduce and publicize how the communists were. If one did not hold on to one's ambitions, one would lose oneself to the bandits. Living in the bandit areas, there was no time when one was not trembling with fear.

Record of Inspection in Bandit Areas 90

At 2:10 PM, the ship arrived at Zoujia Wharf, only ten miles from Honghu, the bandit's nest of He Long, and also one of the main strongholds of the communists, about twenty miles from Bailuoji. The communists had a township government there. After the entire delegation disembarked, a skull was found on the river beach. According to Guo Wenfu, director of the liaison office of the Tenth Army, when he was passing west of Xindi on a foreign ship last year, he often saw corpses floating in the river, and there were countless skulls in the bandit areas. Now they have been buried and cleaned up. This is only one in a thousand. The communists' killings and brutality can be seen. Walking a mile, turning and reaching the town, many houses were burned down by the Communist Party and no one repaired them. There were still communist slogans on the walls, which could be vaguely discerned. There were also two notices, one smaller, with only the words Jianli Ninth District Soviet Government Manufacture, February 9, remaining. The other was larger, with the words Xiang-E-West Provincial Soviet Government printed below. The rest of the slogans, such as "Down with White Imperialism" and "Support the Red Army," were visible everywhere. What is most noteworthy is that the boundaries of the fields were completely indistinguishable, because the equal distribution of farmland had been implemented. A certain Zou Yunxiang, who claimed to be the captain of the Luoshan Anti-Communist Volunteer Corps in the Second District of Jianli, was a strong man in his thirties, wearing a gray cloth military uniform. He said that he had once been forced to join the Communist Party and felt all kinds of pain. Now he has surrendered and organized a security regiment to protect his hometown. On the walls of the security regiment's office were posted surrender slogans, saying "Eliminate the communist party that deceives the gods and destroys the Buddha and does not want ancestors," and "Down with the communist bandits who do not produce and rely solely on struggle to make a living," etc. It was also said that everyone here is surnamed Zou, so it is called Zou You Wharf. His elder brother, Zou Yunfeng, is the owner of the security team. Before the communists came, the entire village had about a thousand people, but now there are only a hundred people. Previously, each family had an average of two cows, but now five families only have one cow. And among the only hundred or so people, most are women, the elderly, and the weak. The strong men have almost all been sacrificed. In the Zou Family Ancestral Hall, almost all are spirit tablets for the dead. The reasons for this are: (1) Half of the strong men were forcibly conscripted by the Red Army and mostly died in battle; (2) Those who were lucky enough to not die mostly fled with the Communist Party and their whereabouts are unknown. Now every family is extremely poor, eating small fennel yams. Previously, they rebuilt small houses from large buildings, but now they are demolishing the large buildings and rebuilding small houses. They cannot maintain their livelihoods. If there is no government relief, they will all become starving ghosts. The words were tearful, which were the true circumstances. According to an old man, the bandits were here for a long time. In August this autumn, after Xu Yuanquan's troops from the Tenth Army of the Central Government arrived, they confiscated more than 10,000 guns from the bandits here and killed countless bandits. At that time, corpses were everywhere and the scene was too horrible to bear. Yanglingji is located to the west of the village, facing Ma'anshan, which belongs to Linxiang County. It is also a base for the communists. There is a Dongyue Temple on the shore, which has now been destroyed.

Walking Twenty Miles 91

On the night of the 6th, the Wan'an wheel stopped forty miles from Bailuoji because the river water was shallow and not suitable for sailing at night. At 10:30 AM on the morning of the 7th, the ship arrived at Shangche Bay, and most of the delegation disembarked here. Shangche Bay is a small town, and the embankment is called Crescent Embankment. The old embankment has almost completely collapsed, and the new embankment is solid. The entire delegation walked along the embankment. Every few hundred steps, there was a thatched shed, and outside the shed stood five or six strong villagers, carrying large swords and holding red spears, saying that they were the local spear teams protecting the area, with a total of about 800 people. People passing by here had to be checked. Those who had passes and good citizen certificates could avoid being checked. Trenches, barbed wire, and bamboo nails were dug on the embankment. It was heard that two months ago, they were still facing the bandit army across the river, so the defense was extremely strict. The members of the delegation walked on the embankment for 25 miles to reach Jianli City. County Chief Zhou and Zhu Shaobo, the deputy head of the security regiment, led a team to greet them. The members of the delegation briefly had tea and snacks in the thatched huts on the riverbank. Then, because the ship was aground in the shallow water on the river bank twelve miles from Jianli, small boats were borrowed to carry the members of the delegation to the Wan'an wheel, and the Wan'an wheel was dragged out of danger. At 3:30 PM, the ship started to return to Hankou. At 6:00 PM, it berthed on the river surface 120 miles from Jianli. At that time, a Japanese warship was also berthed here. On the morning of the 8th, the ship set sail eastward and arrived in Hankou at 7:00 PM.

Japanese Consul's Explanation 92

The survey team is scheduled to depart by car at 8:00 AM on the 10th to Yuekou, and then take a shallow-draft boat downstream from Yuekou to survey the embankment works along the Xiang River. It is planned to return to Hankou on the 12th, transfer to the Ping-Han train northward, and inspect the embankment works in Zhengzhou, Luoyang, and other places. Also, the Japanese Consul General in Hankou, Shimizu Yaichi, specifically went to the Yangtze River Hotel on the morning of the 9th to visit Simpson, the vice-chairman of the Flood Relief Association. Zhou Qibang and Lin Shiliang met with him on his behalf. In addition to explaining in writing the reasons why the embankment works in the Japanese concession had not been completed, the Japanese consul verbally stated that the reason why the embankment works had been delayed was because the budget had not been approved by Tokyo. Now he has received a telegram from Tokyo approving an increase in the embankment construction funds of 78,000 yuan, so it is planned to start embankment construction in February next spring. As for the Embankment Construction Committee of the concession, it will cooperate with the National Government Flood Relief Association in every way. (Qian Hua dispatched from Hankou on December 9)

Meeting to Repair the Ancient Bell Tower in Beiqiao Town 96

Election of Custodial and Works Committee Members

The ancient bell tower of Mingxin Temple in Beiqiao Town, Shanghai County, was built in the Five Dynasties and is the oldest building in the region. It was repaired during the reign of Emperor Qianlong of the Qing Dynasty. It is now on the verge of collapse, and local people have planned to initiate repairs. Yesterday noon, County Chief Yan invited initiators from various places to discuss the matter at the Dadong Restaurant. More than forty people attended, including Wang Yiting, Chu Minyi, Zhao Jinqing, Gao Tie'an, Zheng Yuxiu, Huang Ruisheng, Shen Menglian, Huang Yunseng, Yao Xin, and Li Jinhou. At the scene, all the initiators pledged large sums of money and agreed to raise funds separately, ensuring that the ancient relics are preserved and the appearance is renewed. At the same time, Wang Yiting, Huang Ruisheng, and Yang Nianchun were elected as members of the donation custody committee, and Sun Shengzeng, Sun Siben, He Xinyu, Yin Lisheng, and Shen Buying were elected as members of the works committee, so as to be responsible for carrying out the work separately. The collection point was designated as the West Gate Shanghai Bank, and the deadline for ending the donation was before the solar new year. According to County Chief Yan, in the future repair plan, in addition to preserving the advantages of the original architectural style, some land will be set aside next to it to arrange a simple park, which is planned to be named Mingxin Park, as a place for the residents to rest.

Wu Guangzong Assassination Case 97

The Criminals are Taken to the District Court

Wu Guangzong, the director of the Naval Survey Bureau, was assassinated at his residence in Ningkang Lane, West Gate. After the incident, the City Public Security Bureau arrested Zhou Mingshan, Wu Jigui, Zhang Changlin, Zhang Shaoliang, Song Jiande, Wang Acai, Yao Jiechen, Zou Hongshan, and eight other people, and presented them to the Military Law Department of the Garrison Command for research. Because the investigation determined that this case was under the jurisdiction of ordinary justice, the First Regiment of the Gendarmerie was ordered to dispatch a platoon of soldiers to transfer them to the District Court for trial yesterday.

Shocking Case of Rape and Death of a Young Girl 98

Four-Year-Old Girl's Lower Body Ruptured

Died Two Days Later

A woman named Jiang Mao in Traffic Lane No. 20, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, had a daughter named Jiang Xiaozhu, who was four years old. She was very clever, like a small bird clinging to her mother, and everyone liked her very much. Hu Liao, the wife of Hu Xuan Ting, a Jiangbei native living in the back building, loved the girl very much and often had her sleep with them. Hu also loved her. About a month ago, Hu and his wife were sleeping in the same bed with the child in between them. After some intimate conversation, they began to play with the child. Unexpectedly, Hu Xuan Ting had a curious urge and raped the child. Considering that a four or five-year-old child's reproductive system is not yet fully developed, how could she withstand such abuse? This led to a rupture of her lower body, causing fatal injuries and profuse bleeding. The next morning, Jiang Mao discovered what had happened and immediately filed a complaint against the Hu couple at the Second Precinct of the Fifth District, who were then handed over to the local court for investigation. Little Pearl died two days later. The court sent the body to the Forensic Examination Office of the Ministry of Justice in Zhenru for examination, which confirmed that she had died from rape injuries. The prosecutor then charged Hu Xuan Ting and Hu Liao with the crimes of rape and aiding and abetting rape resulting in death and filed a public indictment. The court session was held the other day by Judge Shen, but the defendants firmly denied the charges, claiming that Jiang Mao was trying to extort money through false accusations. The judge stated that the facts had already been established and there was a forensic report to prove it, so there was no room for denial. He then declared the debate closed and adjourned for sentencing. The defendants were taken back into custody.

Anticipated Celebration of Madam Wang Zhengting's Eightieth Birthday 99

January 10th marks the eightieth birthday of Madam Wang Zhengting, mother of Central Committee member and National Government Committee member Wang Zhengting. It is still remembered that ten years ago, the celebration of her seventieth birthday was held at the Ningbo Association in Shanghai, with many people offering congratulations. The Wang family has five brothers; Zhengting is the third. The second brother passed away early, and the eldest brother died this spring. The fourth and fifth brothers are both engaged in industry and commerce and often travel to different places. When the Second Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee closed, Jiang Jieshi and Wang Jingwei telegraphed Wang Zhengting, seeking his consent to serve as envoy to England. He replied that he had an elderly mother at home and could not travel far. This time, he originally intended to hold a celebration, but due to the current national crisis, his mother instructed him not to be extravagant. No invitations will be sent, and only a family banquet will be held. The thousand yuan saved from the banquet will be donated to charity. Gifts from the outside, such as screens, banners, and couplets, will be politely declined as they would only waste resources. If friends and relatives wish to offer congratulatory gifts, the money will also be donated to disaster relief efforts. It is reported that the Fuxu Road Liuhegou Coal Mining Company is handling the matter on his behalf.

Ningbo Association Requests Maintenance of Chen Limei's Property Rights 101

The Ningbo Association in Shanghai sent a letter to the Yin County government yesterday regarding the auction of Chen Limei's property by the former Ningbo Shatien Branch. The letter stated: "According to the letter from our fellow townsman Chen Limei, Limei purchased a piece of land measuring 1.254 mu located in front of the old Xu Family Gate in Jiaodong, Yin County, in July of the 14th year of the Republic [1925], on which seven single-story houses were built. He holds an imprinted deed and registration certificates No. 1089 from the Zhejiang Shatien Bureau of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government and No. 134 from the Ningbo Municipal Government Land Registration Office. Furthermore, in July of the 20th year of the Republic [1931], the former Ningbo Shatien Branch re-measured the land and found no excess. He holds the branch's preliminary measurement slip, Ningzi No. 771. Unexpectedly, in September of this year, the branch illegally auctioned the land. He has repeatedly stated his reasons and petitioned the Zhejiang Shatien Bureau for legal remedies, but has been rejected. He has no choice but to ask for help and has attached a document requesting the county government to forward it to the bureau. Chen Limei purchased the land eight years ago, holds grain certificates, and has built houses and managed the property. The branch should not, under the pretext of overdue registration and payment, arbitrarily dispose of the property. Based on the foregoing, we respectfully submit the original petition and request your review and prompt legal remedy to protect the property rights, which would be deeply appreciated."

Whereabouts of Three Students Unknown 102

Families Urgently Seek Information

He Qinglan from Xuhui Public School in Xujiahui, Shanghai, Zhang Fuxiang from Suzhou, and Yao Zhenfu from Zhangjiaqiao, Pudong, all sixteen years old, are classmates and close friends. In addition to searching everywhere, they have printed leaflets and distributed them to all sectors of society. Anyone who can find the three students will be rewarded with 100 yuan in cash to reunite them with their families. Their parents are very worried and have sent people to search in various places.

Special Alert in the Chinese Concession Yesterday 104

Peaceful and Normal All Day

According to the National News Agency, yesterday (the 11th) was the anniversary of the Communist Party's Guangzhou Uprising. The authorities in this city received a confidential report that a large number of Communists were hiding in various factories, inciting ignorant workers and unemployed laborers to petition various Party and government agencies in the Chinese Concession and seize the opportunity to riot. After receiving the report, the Municipal Public Security Bureau ordered all district precincts to be especially vigilant. In addition to deploying double guards at all key locations, the inspectors and detectives of the Inspectorate and Detective Team were dispatched to conduct inspections of pedestrians in coordination with the officers of each district precinct and to maintain strict vigilance. Therefore, the city was exceptionally peaceful, and no incidents occurred.

Communists Attempt to Destroy Russian Shanghai Newspaper 105

Fourteen Arrested

According to the Zi Lin Daily, on the night of yesterday (the 10th), there were again communist rioters, who were allegedly plotting to destroy the Shanghai Newspaper, a Russian newspaper in this city. Fourteen Chinese were arrested by the French Concession police. Bricks, glass bottles, and yellow sand were found in their bags. It is said that there have been two previous attempts to attack the newspaper this year. On August 6th, several Chinese communists smashed two panes of glass in the newspaper's windows. Three were arrested by nearby patrol officers. Yesterday, there was a second attempt, and they brought yellow sand, attempting to destroy the newspaper's printing and typesetting machines. The French police received a tip-off in advance, stating that they were planning to act at 11:00 AM. In the morning, they dispatched a large number of detectives in disguise to guard the vicinity of the newspaper office. Perhaps the rioters saw the detectives in disguise and became suspicious, so they did not act immediately. However, the detectives continued to monitor them without懈怠. Until 7:00 PM, a group of pedestrians suddenly appeared. The detectives surrounded them and, after a brief confrontation, arrested fourteen people. Bricks, glass bottles, and yellow sand were found on their persons, and they were taken back to the police station for questioning. It is reported that they were all dressed as students.

Starting from New Year's Day of the 22nd Year, Traditional Chinese Medicine Prescriptions Will Use the New Weights and Measures System 108

The Right Side of the Prescription Will Be Stamped with the Words "New Scale"

One Old Guan Liang Equals 1.1730 New Liangs

Regarding the case of the Shanghai medical and pharmaceutical industries adopting the new weights and measures system (i.e., the municipal scale), the Social Affairs Bureau previously ordered the National Industry Trade Association to deliberate and respond. The industry subsequently decided to implement the system starting from January 1, 1933. The Social Affairs Bureau then sent a letter to the Education Bureau, instructing various medical organizations to comply at the same time. After receiving the order, the medical organizations in this city repeatedly consulted and discussed the matter, and agreed on a conversion table for the old and new scales, which they submitted to the Municipal Education Bureau. It is now learned that all the traditional Chinese medicine practitioners in this city have decided to comply with the order. Starting from New Year's Day next year, prescriptions will use the quantities in the table and be verified accordingly, and the right side of the prescription will be stamped with a wooden seal that says "The above-mentioned medicines are all new scale." A reporter from the New Voice News believes that this matter is very important as it relates to patients taking medicine. Sometimes patients prepare one or two medicines themselves from traditional Chinese medicine prescriptions. The conversion method of the old and new weights and measures must be detailed and clear to avoid mistakes. He specifically inquired with the Shenzhou National Medical Association and obtained the conversion table and explanation as follows:

Conversion: Cao Ping One He Equals 1.173 Municipal Scale

0.1.5 He Equals 1.7595 Municipal Scale, 2 He

Equals 2.3460 Municipal Scale, 2.5 He Equals 2.932

5 Municipal Scale, 3 He Equals 3.5190 Municipal Scale, 3.5 He Equals

4.1055 Municipal Scale, 4 He Equals 4.6920, 4

.5 He Equals 5.2785 Municipal Scale, 5 He Equals 5.8

651, 5.5 He Equals 6.4516, 6 He

Equals 7.0281, 6.5 He Equals 7.6246, 7 He Equals 8.2111, 7.5 He Equals 8.7976, 8 He Equals 9.3841, 8.5 He Equals 9.9706, 9 He Equals 10.5571, 9.5 He Equals 11.1436,

Explanation: (1) This table is based on the regulations of the city-use system promulgated by the National Government. Cao Ping is the Shanghai 16-liang balance scale. Each jin or liang equals the city jin or liang (1.1730) conversion. (2) For the convenience of our medical community, we have briefly described it. According to the old system, one jin of Cao Ping is divided into sixteen liangs, and the new system also stipulates that one city jin is also sixteen liangs. Therefore, the ratio between jin and jin and the ratio between liang and liang are both (1.1730). (3) One liang of the old Cao Ping equals 1.1730 of the new system. The (1730) after the decimal point can be called one qian seven fen three li. Because after liang, everything is in decimal increments. But at the same time, because the city jin is still sixteen liangs, the (1) before the decimal point should be one jin, and the (1730) after the decimal point represents one-tenth of (1730) jin, which should be multiplied by sixteen to get (2768), which is two liang seven qian six fen eight li. If you ask how many new systems one jin of the old system equals, you should answer one jin two liang seven qian six fen eight li. (4) According to the amount used by our medical community, such as one fen, half a fen, two fen, one qian, half a qian, two qian, to one liang, half a liang, two liang, this table is simple, but it is enough to apply. One liang of the old Cao Ping equals one liang one qian seven fen three li of the new municipal system, and one qian of Cao Ping equals one qian one fen seven li three hao of the new system. Because the ratios listed in this table are all ratios, there is no fixed unit. What kind of unit it is depends on the unit of the old system when it is applied. (5) The above is about converting from the old system to the new system. If converting from the new system to the old system, divide (1) by (1.1730) to get (8525), which is a 8525% discount. Multiply sixteen liang of the new municipal system by (8525) to get thirteen liang six qian four fen of the old Cao Ping, which is also mentioned for the sake of clarity, but it is not actually needed, so no separate table is made.

Request for Protection of the Han Mausoleum 110

To Preserve the Lives of the People of Mengjin

The Shanghai Fundraising Association for Disaster Relief in Henan, Anhui, and Hubei received a letter yesterday from Mr. Li Huanying, a member of the Relief Committee, stating:

Respectfully informing, I have observed that the old course of the Yellow River in Mengjin County, located about twenty-odd li north of the county seat, offers a wide and open view from the northern Mang Mountains, with beautiful scenery, being the birthplace of civilization since ancient times. However, since the early Qing Dynasty, when the river shifted southward, the riverbanks have gradually collapsed, and recently, they have even encroached upon the mountains, and countless villages and farmlands have been submerged by the vast waters. Fortunately, due to the presence of the mausoleum of Emperor Guangwu of the Han Dynasty, the nation has repeatedly allocated funds to construct stone dams, allowing the mausoleum and temples to be maintained, and providing protection for the people. Unexpectedly, on the 10th and 12th of August this year, the river waters rose dramatically twice, causing hundreds of zhang of the riverbank upstream of the Han Mausoleum to collapse, and the riverbed became silted up, as high as the bank, with the old embankment submerged in mud, losing its function. If the water rises again next year, flooding will be unstoppable, and there is a concern that the mausoleum and temples will be submerged. Emperor Guangwu was brave, benevolent, and brought about the restoration of the dynasty, being a rare and exemplary ruler after the Three Dynasties in our country. Later generations, cherishing the memory of his achievements, still wish to protect and glorify the deteriorating mausoleum and the dilapidated temples. However, protecting the mausoleum requires preventing river damage first. If the resting place of the emperor were to be turned into the lair of the River God, it would not only be a laughingstock to both domestic and foreign observers but also cause unease in people's hearts. Moreover, the tens of li of city and people in the eastern half of Mengjin County will soon be submerged, which is also a cause for compassion among benevolent gentlemen. Previously, I accompanied Mr. Dai Jitao and Mr. Wang Yiting on a visit to the Han Mausoleum, where we witnessed the perilous situation. The local gentry and people have long harbored hidden worries, and when discussing the danger of river disasters and the calamity of submersion, they were almost in tears. Mr. Dai and Mr. Wang were also deeply moved and considered ways to prevent this major disaster from happening. I have long admired your association's efforts in reviving what has fallen into disuse, upholding morality and justice, saving people from fire and drowning, and benefiting all living beings. Your benevolent heart and reputation are universally admired. Agricultural Society and Other Groups Oppose Jiangsu Province's Abolition of the Department of Industry 112

The Jiangsu Agricultural Society and other groups sent a telegram yesterday to the Central Political Council, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Industry, stating: To the esteemed Central Political Council of Nanjing, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Industry: The Jiangsu Provincial Government suddenly decided to abolish the Department of Industry at the provincial government meeting on the 6th, merging it into the Department of Construction. We do not know on what laws of the National Government this is based. According to the Provincial Government Organization Law, the Central Political Council decides on the establishment or abolition of departments and the appointment or removal of committee members, which is submitted to the Executive Yuan and presented to the National Government for orders. Now, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, located near the seat of the National Government, can abolish a department and remove committee members with just a committee, replacing the functions and powers of the Central Political Council and the Executive Yuan. If this precedent is set, it will inevitably lead to a situation of warlord separatism, making it difficult for central government orders to leave the capital, endangering the nation's position to an extreme degree. At the government meeting on the 9th, all provincial and county farms were uniformly suspended and personnel were dispatched for safekeeping. Since unification and return to the provinces, Jiangsu's agricultural administration has been on the right track, and the promotion of improvements has reached a certain scale. Local agricultural funding has increased to over 800,000 yuan, progressing in an orderly manner, and the results are becoming increasingly apparent. Enlightened individuals feel the importance of the food problem, establishing agricultural villages, giving lectures on promotion, striving to improve, and fearing being too late. Now, funding has been reduced to over 200,000 yuan, which is already severely damaging. Now, it is being completely abolished, and countless industries will be abandoned, and years of experimentation will be completely destroyed. This means that Jiangsu's agriculture, sericulture, cotton, fishery, animal husbandry, forestry, and mining will never have a chance to improve. Moreover, China is a nation founded on agriculture, and Jiangsu's wealth ranks first in the Southeast, relying on sericulture, rice, cotton, and fishing. There is no time to improve and maintain them. Once abolished, it is tantamount to digging one's own grave and destroying the foundation of the nation. The esteemed council, the executive yuan, and departments issue orders, supervise and direct, and have specialized responsibilities. We request that you promptly correct its illegality in accordance with the law, strictly order the cessation of its merger, and quickly restore the agricultural organizations that maintain the people's food supply, benefiting the farmers of Jiangsu and safeguarding the foundation of the nation. We cannot express our urgency and await your command. Sincerely, the Jiangsu Agricultural Society, Jiangsu Poultry Society, Jiangsu Beekeeping Society, Jiangsu Sericulture Society, Jiangbei Reclamation Promotion Association, Reclamation Research Society, and Jiangsu Rural Improvement Association.

Page 13

Talk by Gu Mengyu, Minister of Railways 113

The Zhenru Joint Transportation Station Plan

After the January 28th Incident, all buildings and equipment at the Shanghai North Station were destroyed by artillery fire. The Ministry of Railways has established a committee to plan and revive the construction of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways. It is reported that the plan is to set up a joint transportation station in Zhenru and a passenger terminal in Jiangwan. Recently, due to land use issues, local farmers, whose fields and houses have already suffered significant losses after the war, fear that their remaining land and houses will be requisitioned, leaving them with nothing to live on, and have been requesting exemptions. Reporters stationed in Beijing believe that this matter is of great importance to the revival of Shanghai's economy, and members of the community want to know the content of this plan. Recently, Gu Mengyu, Minister of Railways, returned to Beijing from Hankou, and reporters visited Mr. Gu at the Ministry of Railways to inquire about everything. He graciously received them immediately and gave the following answers. Below are the reporter's questions and Mr. Gu's answers.

Necessary Circumstances 114

(Question) Your ministry is reviving the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo railways, and it is said that a joint transportation station will be set up in Zhenru and a passenger terminal in Jiangwan. What are the necessary circumstances for this? (Answer) The Shanghai Municipal Government previously promulgated the Shanghai Municipal Central Area Plan, proposing to set up a passenger terminal next to the West Zhongshan North Road in the city center, and a freight terminal to be moved out of the city along the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, to the outskirts near Zhenru. It also believes that the existing North Station obstructs the traffic in Zhabei and advocates for its relocation. The ministry, considering the development of the municipality and the welfare of the public, and recognizing that the railway itself does indeed need to be relocated, decided to build a joint transportation station at the west of the intersection of Zhongshan Road and Jiaotong Road, occupying land on both the north and south sides of the current railway line, namely within the Zhenru and Pengpu areas. The passenger terminal will be set up in Jiangwan. (Question) After the war, vitality has not yet been restored. Why not simply restore the old appearance of the North Station on its original site and instead undertake such large-scale construction at this time? (Answer) The development of Shanghai's economy is extremely rapid. The existing station was planned thirty years ago. Compared to thirty years ago, Shanghai's population has increased and its commerce has prospered, making it vastly different. In terms of its location and facilities, it is no longer sufficient to meet current needs and must be relocated sooner or later. However, without the losses of war, it might still be possible to make do and muddle through. This destruction, although an extremely tragic and unfortunate event, is actually a new opportunity in terms of construction. Because the original station will eventually be forced by the general trend to relocate to a better location. If we temporarily follow the old ways, the losses from demolition and reconstruction after future repairs will be even greater. Therefore, it is better to resolutely and decisively take this opportunity to plan carefully and make a permanent solution. On the one hand, it can promote the progress of the railway and facilitate passenger and freight transport, and on the other hand, it can assist the development of the municipality and increase the welfare of the people.

Significance of Site Selection 115

(Question) Then what is the significance of choosing the location? (Answer) As mentioned earlier, the original North Station is not sufficient to meet current needs. Therefore, in order to remedy this deficiency and to adequately replace the North Station, the most suitable location is the sparsely populated area on the west side of Shanghai, which is convenient for the loading and unloading of passengers and freight, and is also close to the North Station. Therefore, the selection of the location and the design of the station are based on three principles: (1) It cannot be too far from the center of Shanghai; (2) The two railways must be conveniently connected, without losing their connection; (3) The future terminal must be set up in Jiangwan, taking into account the convenience of direct access to the terminal. Question: What is the design situation like? (Answer) The track layout of the North Station has always been difficult for trains to navigate, with many twists and turns. Since the joint transportation station has been decided, the current passenger trains will certainly use it as their terminus. However, after the passenger terminal is built in the future, there will be even more trains passing through. Therefore, this joint transportation station is designed according to the scale of a through station. The track layout includes many passing tracks, and each line is designed to be economical and practical. The facilities of the platforms and station buildings are mainly for the convenience of passengers. Also, in order to reduce shunting time, the locomotive shed and carriage shed are properly arranged so that after the train is unloaded at the platform, it can drive straight into the carriage shed. The locomotive can then drive forward from the carriage shed, pass through a curve, turn around, and drive into the locomotive shed. In the future, when the train departs for the return journey, it will not need to turn the locomotive around again. Once the design was finalized, the current selected location was chosen.

Area Occupied 116

(Question) Approximately how much land will the new plan occupy? (Answer) The area of land occupied is approximately 2,800 mu, of which approximately 150 mu are occupied by the roadbed, and the rest is necessary for track layout and various buildings. (Question) Why is so much land occupied? (Answer) The increase in railway business in recent years, the rapid development of Shanghai in the future, and the prosperity of the port will all progress rapidly. This plan is designed to meet the needs of the next fifty years, so the scale must be somewhat expanded. Furthermore, to facilitate passengers and merchants, in addition to the aforementioned station buildings, tracks, carriage sheds, and locomotive sheds, all freight yards, various offices, railway hotels, staff dormitories, and other railway-related buildings are arranged near the station buildings. Therefore, everything is considered to improve the work efficiency of employees and the convenience of business travelers. Therefore, this joint transportation station cannot be regarded as a current plan, and the land purchased is determined according to the required scope.

Land Purchase Procedures 117

(Question) What are the procedures for demarcating the area and purchasing the land? (Answer) The ministry's purchase of this land is a national transportation undertaking, and all procedures should be carried out in accordance with the Land Expropriation Law promulgated and implemented by the National Government. (Question) How will the land be priced, and how will compensation be given for the attachments on the land? (Answer) The most fair land price will naturally be given for the land used. For the attachments on the land used, such as houses, graves, green crops, and trees, a corresponding relocation fee will also be given. At that time, the ministry will return to the Shanghai Municipal Government to investigate the local situation and will propose various prices and announce them in detail, consulting with the land owners to complete the purchase. (Question) What are the procedures for issuing land prices and relocation fees? (Answer) The ministry aims to make it convenient for the land owners. Once the price has been agreed upon, it is only necessary to complete the procedures for proving ownership before issuing the price.

Request to Higher Authorities 118

(Question) Currently, the villagers in the Zhenru expropriation zone are fiercely opposed. How will your ministry respond? (Answer) The railway construction plan aims to facilitate transportation for the entire society. Its focus is naturally different from the narrow-minded self-interest of individuals. We are very sympathetic to the losses of the farmers in Zhenru, such as flowers, gardens, and trees, which affect their lives. We will naturally do our best to find ways to alleviate their pain. In the event that the resistance is too great, and some members of society are unable to understand, rendering the ministry unable to achieve a comprehensive solution, then we will have no choice but to submit it to the higher authorities of the ministry to decide on a solution.

Wu Chao-Shu's Talk 119

Advising the People of the Nation Not to Rely On or Be Dissatisfied with the League of Nations

The Only Way to Resolve the National Crisis Is to Strive for Self-Strengthening

Yesterday, a reporter from the New Sound News visited Dr. Wu Chao-Shu, a member of the Central Committee, at his private residence and asked him to express his views on the League of Nations and how to deal with diplomacy. He said that he made a detailed observation and analysis of the League of Nations at the Peace Conference last year, because the League of Nations itself was not established for long, and it did not have the strength to sanction violence. It also made pleasing powerful nations its daily task. Therefore, it is extravagant to hope that it will have a good result for the Sino-Japanese dispute. In other words, if the League of Nations had the power to sanction violence, it would not have wanted to uphold justice. The resolution passed last year would have been implemented long ago. Therefore, the meetings and discussions of the League of Nations only serve to prolong the time, waiting for China to strive for its own liberation during this time. Therefore, the people of the nation should no longer rely on or be dissatisfied with the League of Nations, but should strengthen their military, enrich their internal affairs, increase their strength to resist Japan, and seek a new path of self-strengthening to resolve the national crisis.

Reader's Advisor 121

A letter from Mr. Chang Chunsheng: I am a high school student who is about to graduate. Every day, I am busy with classes at school, listening to the indoctrination-style lectures of the teachers and reading mechanical textbooks, which makes me feel very bored. Looking at our country and society, corruption is rampant to an extreme degree. Foreign troubles are increasing, and the affairs of the nation remain the same. The corruption of society is getting worse day by day. It is truly hopeless! In this situation, I cannot see anyone who can truly take on the responsibility of saving the country and the people and purifying society. The future is truly unimaginable! In this situation, I truly feel the meaninglessness of life. Life is full of pain and has no joy. The future has no hope. What is the point of studying? I truly want to escape this corrupt society and this hopeless country! I truly do not know what I should do! Your newspaper is the guide for the people of the whole country. The gentlemen are knowledgeable and experienced. You are willing to take the time to guide young people who are as troubled as I am. Therefore, I dare to ask for your guidance, hoping that you will not abandon me and teach me. That would be very fortunate!

Reply: According to your letter, there are two reasons why you are feeling troubled. One is because you do not feel interested in the "indoctrination-style lectures" and "mechanical textbooks." The other is because you feel that "the country and society are corrupt and rotten" and that "nothing can be done." Your ability to feel this kind of trouble has already proven that you are a thoughtful young person, at least not a person who is simply living in a drunken dream. You are already looking for a way out. We believe that in your constant search, you will definitely find the right path.

Examining the two reasons that are causing you trouble, the former is very simple. Perhaps the instructor's method is not effective and cannot arouse the interest of the students, or perhaps you have your own thoughts and do not feel interested in the rigid classroom life. But the blame does not lie in the "mechanical nature of the textbooks." If you can use the mechanical textbooks in a lively way and integrate knowledge and action, in other words, if you use your brain in the classroom and then use your hands to experiment outside the classroom, you will definitely realize that "textbooks" are not "mechanical" and that "studying is not a "hard thing."

Regarding the latter, this is naturally a very serious problem facing our nation. Internal strife and foreign troubles are tormenting us. In this situation, I think that as long as one is not willing to live in a drunken dream, there is no one who does not deeply feel pain and trouble.

However, we believe that this problem cannot be solved by feeling troubled. Trouble can only kill yourself and plunge our nation into greater darkness and hopelessness. At the same time, we also believe that only the brave are willing to stand in front of the problem, and only the brave can seek answers from the problem. As long as the Chinese people are willing to stand in front of the problem and not avoid it, and are also willing to seek answers from the problem, then China will definitely not be without hope. Even Korea and India, whose countries have been destroyed and whose people have been enslaved, their surviving remnants of their perished nations have not given up hope for their countries and are still constantly fighting. How much more is this true for our country, which has not yet fallen into the tragic situation of Korea and India?

You are a young person, and also a student youth. You are the future master of our country. In other words, the problems of our country are placed on your shoulders. There is no way, you must think of a way. There is no way out, you must think of a way out. You should not avoid the problem, you should not shirk responsibility, you should not wait for others. Troubled? Trouble can only kill yourself and send our country on a path of death that is truly unsolvable.

Therefore, no matter what, you should not be troubled. Stand bravely in front of the problem, find a way out of the difficulties, there are many people seeking a way out, as long as you have the determination, you will definitely find your companions.

When there is "truly no way," there will "be a way." History will not deceive people. Why are you troubled?

A letter from Mr. Gao Qian'an: In recent years, the morals of the world have deteriorated day by day, and morality has declined. News of rape, murder, theft, and adultery fills the newspapers, almost making people suspect that newspapers are specifically published to record the evils of society. Looking back on the past, in times of chaos and famine, there were also many cases of murder, robbery, and fighting, but the world has never been filled with bandits as much as it is today. The reason for this is the harm caused by the abandonment of ritual education and the prevalence of evil theories. The loyal gentlemen of today only know how to call and run around to resist insults and save the nation, but they do not know that the morals of the world and the hearts of the people are like this, the lifeblood of the country has been cut off, and even without the arrival of strong bandits, it will eventually perish. Without understanding the fundamentals, their actions will be ineffective. Therefore, in my opinion, saving the nation must start with saving the morals of the world and the hearts of the people, and the rope and discipline of ritual education are especially critical to survival. Otherwise, even if one has the power to turn the tide, it will eventually be futile. Do you gentlemen think so? Your newspaper is the leader of society and has the responsibility of correcting the hearts of the people. I deeply hope that your newspaper will lead the way in saving this decadent world.

Reply: Your letter expresses great concern about the worsening of the morals of the world and the hearts of the people today, and the world being filled with bandits, which is a feeling that we all share. However, I cannot agree with your letter's attribution of the cause to the abandonment of ritual education and the prevalence of evil theories, and your desire to maintain the rope and discipline of ritual education as a way to save the morals of the world and the hearts of the people and to save the country in danger. The ancients once said: "If the people are rich, they cannot be employed with emoluments; if they are poor, they cannot be punished with punishments. The laws are not enforced, and the people are not well-governed, because of the inequality of wealth." It is also said: "In all ways of governing a country, it is necessary to enrich the people first. If the people are rich, they are easy to govern; if the people are poor, they are difficult to govern." "When the granaries are full, they know etiquette; when they are well-fed and clothed, they know honor and shame." It can be seen that the reason why China has become a bandit world today is because "the people cannot make a living," not because of the prevalence of evil theories. Modern sociologists who study the source of evil mostly attribute it to economic relations. Even those that are due to heredity are caused by society. Therefore, it is not only murder and robbery that are caused by the oppression of life, but also other crimes are due to the bad social system. The prevalence of evil proves the bankruptcy of society and the exhaustion of the people's livelihood. Therefore, we are deeply concerned about the morals of the world and the hearts of the people in China today, but what we should focus on is not the latter but the former. If we do not investigate the true cause and only lament the rope and discipline of ritual education, we are truly abandoning the root and pursuing the branch, and we will only have lamentation forever.
