[Educational News Highlights: Su Education Commissioner Zhou Fohai Inspects Northern Jiangsu (8) L]

Visited Rugao Middle School in the morning and gave a lengthy talk.

Convened a meeting with the entire city's education community in the evening.

(Rugao Correspondent) This morning, on the 7th, at 8:00 AM, Education Commissioner Zhou Fohai and his party continued their educational inspection. They first went to Rugao County Middle School, where Principal Xu guided them on a tour of the school's facilities and observed classes such as geometry and Chinese language. Mr. Zhou inspected and provided guidance one by one, and then went to inspect everything in the school's girls' division. At 11:00 AM, they went to Anding Elementary School to inspect the teaching of children at all levels in great detail and provided many instructions. They returned to their residence for lunch at noon (because they declined all social engagements). At 2:00 PM in the afternoon, they went to Rugao Middle School to give a speech, stating that Rugao Normal School is a provincial school and should strive to be a model for all public and private schools. Regarding the three aspects of discipline, thought, and level, efforts should be made to improve them. The direction of improvement lies in seeking personal survival and serving society in order to cultivate truly useful talents. There are three conditions for this: first, rich knowledge; second, a sound personality; and third, correct thinking. Mr. Zhou explained these three aspects in great detail and elaborated on them thoroughly, and said that students must study and must have real knowledge in order to resist Japan and save the country. He also stated that Rugao customs are prone to litigation, and the education community often engages in anonymous posters, which is not a bright and upright attitude. In the future, students should be careful not to contract this bad habit. The spirit of national virtues such as loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, peace, and so on should be promoted and the spirit of the great country should be carried forward. It is also necessary to obey the orders of teachers, abide by discipline, value order, and restore the true view of respecting teachers and valuing the Way. He cited the deeds and learning style of Hu Angong, a great Confucian scholar of the Song Dynasty in Rugao, as an example, and encouraged them. Finally, he corrected the psychology of arrogance in senior students and deeply repented of the reckless release of ideas by normal school students. In the future, school management must adopt strict doctrines. Teachers and staff can strictly manage students. If teachers and staff can strictly manage students, then they will be good teachers and students, and students can receive strict management from teachers and staff. The explanation was thorough and detailed, and all 300 teachers and students present were moved. The speech lasted for one and a half hours before it ended. Principal Shen led them to the playground for a group photo. That night at 8:00 PM, he went to the county party headquarters auditorium to convene a meeting with the education community of the entire city. More than 200 people attended. Mr. Zhou said that Rugao education has three undesirable phenomena: first, factions; second, lack of funding; and third, lack of vitality, that is, chaos, poverty, theft, and exhaustion. The reorganization of Rugao education is nothing more than planning, funding, and talent, three points. (1) In terms of planning, do not aim too high or be overly ambitious, but be realistic and able to achieve it. The Education Bureau should be ordered to re-formulate a detailed and concrete plan and submit it for review and approval. (2) In terms of funding, there are three methods: one is to increase revenue, the second is to reorganize, and the third is to reduce expenditure. In terms of increasing revenue, the Education Department has already raised overdue fines, which can generate more than 10,000 yuan per year. Miscellaneous donations and land rents can all be reorganized, and taxes should be collected promptly. There are also three ways to reduce expenditure: first, unnecessary agencies and personnel should be laid off with drastic measures; second, redundant positions should be merged; and third, internal measures should be taken to tighten spending. (3) In terms of talent, if A overthrows B and A takes over, it is not possible in fact, and even if it is, it is not good. If they fight each other, they will both be harmed. The best way is to work together to eliminate factions. As for how to reorganize Rugao education, the Education Department will send several supervisors to Rugao to assist the local authorities in implementing it thoroughly. Within three years, Rugao's education will surely be successful. He returned to his residence at 10:30 PM and is scheduled to attend a speech at the County Middle School at 8:00 AM tomorrow (the 8th), and then go to Tangjia Zha to visit the Dasheng Yarn Factory and other places, and then transfer to Shanghai and Beijing that evening to attend the Third Plenary Session.

(4) Physical ability: This refers to innate ability. The relationship between this ability and physical education is the same as the relationship between intelligence and other subjects. However, there is currently no uniform standard for physical ability testing in the physical education field. Most of the tests used by schools are not formulated according to scientific methods. A relatively reliable criterion is the Brace Physical Ability Test (reference), BraceDKMeaurngMolorAbilityASBarnesCoNewYork. However, it is still necessary to have a spirit of research when applying it.

(5) Skills: This refers to the ability acquired through learning. The methods for testing skills can be divided into universal and special types. For example, selecting five, six, or ten natural movements from various sports activities, such as running, jumping, throwing, and throwing, can be used as a universal skill test. Simple machines can also be used for testing, such as physical strength tests. As for special tests, each sport has its own tests. For example, basketball can use the following tests: (1) free throw; (2) accurate shooting, receiving, and passing; (3) dribbling and shooting; (4) free shooting; (5) passing distance. The following are five grading methods, (1) and (2) are absolutely indispensable, and the remaining three should also be fully adopted. If it feels difficult, at least one must be selected. The following three examples are for reference:

(Note) The relationship between grade level and academic performance is very close, but the current general grading method often ignores it. It must be known that this grading standard can also enable each grade to obtain its corresponding teaching results.

(Example 1) Breaking the Ordinary Grade System

Step 1: Divide the students in each grade into two groups, male and female, according to gender.

Step 2: Divide the first-grade boys and girls into groups according to the results of physical examinations. Those who need special corrective activities are divided into one group, called the "Zi" group. Then, the remaining students are divided into "Chou = Yin" groups according to physical ability or skill test, or a combination of the two. Those below 30% or 40% of the whole grade are in the "Chou" group, and the rest are in the "Yin" group.

Step 3: Divide the second and third grade boys and girls according to Step 2, but divide the students who do not need correction into three groups, or those below the lowest 25% or 30% are in the "Chou" group, those above the highest 25% or 30% are in the "Mao" group, and the rest in the middle are in the "Yin" group.

Step 4: Combine the groups divided in Steps 2 and 3. Zi and Zi are combined into Group A, Chou and Chou are combined into Group B, Yin and Yin are combined into Group C, and Mao is Group D. Thus, all the boys and girls in the school are divided into four groups: A, B, C, and D.

Overseas Chinese Schools Approved by the Ministry of Education in the Recent Three Months 127

The registration of overseas Chinese schools used to be handled by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, which was a cumbersome procedure. Since 1929, the administrative regulations for overseas Chinese education managed by consuls have been jointly agreed upon by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Education, and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission. According to the regulations, the establishment of overseas Chinese schools is directly reported to the Ministry of Education by the consul. The Ministry of Education sends a letter to seek the consent of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, and the Ministry of Education directly orders the consulate to approve the registration. Each month, the Ministry of Education informs the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the overseas Chinese schools approved for registration in that month for record. The overseas Chinese schools approved for registration by the Ministry of Education in September, October, and November are listed below:

(1) In September, there were two schools: Zhenhua Elementary School (Ipoh, British Malaya) and Qunying Elementary School (Mangjie, Vietnam). (2) In October, there were two schools: Guangming Elementary School (Penang) and Busan Overseas Chinese Elementary School (Busan). (3) In November, there was one school: Hong Kong Overseas Chinese Middle School (Hong Kong).

Shanghai Municipal Council Cautiously Distributes Subsidies to Private Schools 133

Among the subsidies issued by the Shanghai Municipal Council to private schools in the concession, there is an item for the construction costs of the Hudong Commune. The Health Department and the Finance Department have now notified the Education Department that they are allowed to issue the fees for the first three quarters of this year to improve sanitation conditions. In addition, the subsidies for five schools will be issued after they have moved to suitable school sites, as advocated by the Health Department. Moreover, the Chairman of the Education Committee found that the situations of Jing'an Elementary School and Shanghai Elementary School were similar, so the fees for these two schools will also be temporarily suspended. In addition, there are six schools that the Health Department has reported as not being very satisfactory, but the Health Department has not advocated suspending the subsidies. Therefore, the Chairman of the Education Committee proposed that the fees for these six schools for this quarter should be issued as usual, but at the same time, it was stated that if sanitation conditions are not improved, the payments will be stopped in the next quarter. After discussion, this proposal was passed, and the Director of the Chinese Education Department solemnly informed the principals of the six schools of this intention. The council's proposal has been approved by the Municipal Council Board of Directors.

Letter from Shanghai College 137

Yesterday, Shanghai College sent a letter stating: "Dear Mr. Editor, in today's Education News column of your newspaper, there is a news item about second-year students of the private Shanghai College petitioning against Zhou and refusing to attend classes. After investigation, it was found that the Chinese language teacher for the first year was Mr. Hu Jingzhi. During the period when Mr. Hu was unable to come to school due to illness, he repeatedly asked people to substitute for him. There was indeed a Mr. Zhou. Since December, Mr. Hu has taken another job, and we were unable to retain him, so the general affairs director, Mr. Yang Daohong, concurrently assumed the position. During the change, more than a dozen students were used by others to drop out of school voluntarily, but the class has never been suspended for a single lesson. The so-called second-year class strike is completely fictitious. The students who dropped out of school have been repeatedly disciplined, but they have stubbornly refused to change their minds. We had no choice but to remove them from the school register to maintain discipline. In the past two days, the parents of the students came to the school and pleaded for the revocation of the decision. For the sake of cherishing the studies of young people, the school gave them a chance to reform themselves and allowed them to remain in school under observation. The facts are clear. We are deeply afraid that the public will misunderstand, so we are sending this letter to request a correction and express our gratitude."

8,000 Fans Pleasantly Surprised as Donghua Overwhelms Argyll 145

Jia League Match

Donghua Scores Three Goals First, Argyll Recovers One

Although Argyll Was Defeated, Their Skill Was Indeed Amazing

A Spectacular Performance This Season

The 8,000 fans at the football field yesterday were pleasantly surprised. The Donghua Football Team was in great luck, defeating the Argyll Football Team of the Scottish Army, which had been dominating Shanghai, by a score of 3-1. The score was 2-0 in the first half and 3-0 in the second half before Argyll added a goal. The match was truly a contest between evenly matched opponents, and the outcome depended entirely on luck. However, although Argyll lost, it seemed to be a notch above Donghua in skill. The spectacular performance was the best seen this season. The referee was Ballard.

Donghua Team Lineup:

Zhou Xianyan, Li Ning, Kai Xun'an, Tu Kaiyuan, Feng Yunyou, Wu Youliang, Wan Xianghua, Chen Hongguang, Li Yichen, Chen Jiaqiu, Cao Qiuting

Argyll Lineup:

Henry, Tau, Que Dou, Hai Si, De Yu, Men Hai Shi, Gra Xin, Hughes, Quitte, Krag, Taylor, Hui Lies

Incredibly Spectacular, A Sight to Behold 146

It was expected that elite troops would meet strong opponents and the performance would be exciting. Argyll came to Shanghai as a substitute for Hamed Shah and showed their skills twice. In the first Jia League match, they defeated Lacks 6-2. In the second Skota Cup match, they thrashed Yiling 10-0 in two weeks. Judging from their performance, it was clear that they were not to be trifled with. The advance of their five forwards was as fast as lightning, their passing was skilled and ingenious, and the accuracy of their hooking shots on both wings was rarely seen at sea. Their crosses from both corners were accurate to the millimeter, a sight to behold. The defense was also steady. The only shortcoming was that the backs were occasionally careless and made mistakes. The Western Police team was probably not as good as them. Although they were defeated, it can be said that their luck was bad. The missed scoring opportunities can only be blamed on themselves. In terms of performance, they were still a notch above Donghua.

Good Luck Prevails, Unstoppable 147

Donghua knew the strength of the enemy, so it issued a special order for strict precautions. Although they broke through the enemy's goal twice in the first half, their own goal was almost a place for the enemy to enter and exit at will, with endless turmoil. Fortunately, good luck prevailed, and all dangers were averted. Li Ning defended the left and looked after the right. If he relaxed even slightly, there would have been a disaster. The entire army was unusually careful in its operations, making the performance twice as exciting as in the past, which is evident.

Dangerous, Dangerous with Opportunities Missed 148

Donghua's victory was truly a stroke of good fortune. The front of the goal was surrounded by a tight siege, but the ball could not be scored. After Donghua scored the first goal against Argyll, the enemy forwards launched repeated attacks. Once, Qin Feixu dribbled past Li Ning and passed lightly to the center. Krag shot straight at the goal from three feet away, but the ball went wide and missed. Tu Kaiyuan committed a foul, and Hai Men took a penalty kick, which also flew out of the goal. There were countless other dangerous balls like these. Among Argyll's forwards, there was a left inner, Raymond, who was excellent at both attacking and shooting and had fast feet. He was absent yesterday and replaced by Quitte, otherwise the situation might have been different.

Unexpectedly, They Scored a Goal First 149

Ballard, the strict referee, ordered the kickoff. Within five minutes, Donghua launched several attacks, but all failed. Tu Kaiyuan passed the ball on the left, Wan Xianghua got it and advanced, passing the ball to the center. In this urgent situation, Hai Si eventually lost his footing, and Li Yichen intercepted the ball and kicked it hard, the ball was strong enough, and it went into the net. Donghua opened the scoring first, and the fans exploded with cheers that had not been heard for a long time.

Overjoyed, Penalty Kick Missed 150

The Scottish army counterattacked, but although the attack was fierce, the defense was also strict, and they could not get close to the goal. When Taylor Hui Lies passed the ball, he was forced to clear the ball, which happened to fall in front of the goal. They held on for three or four minutes before finally getting out of danger, which was also fortunate. However, the enemy's momentum was still strong, and the right wing was even more valiant, constantly probing the border. After another corner kick, Hui Lies got the ball on the right corner and advanced towards the goal. Tu Kaiyuan went to defend, and his hand touched the ball. Like a bolt from the blue, an unexpected penalty kick was awarded. Hai Shi kicked it, and the Scottish army had tried to score several times, knowing the iron gate's skill. The ball went to the right, turning ingenuity into clumsiness, and went out of the goal. The Donghua players hugged each other in great joy, almost going crazy.

A Sudden Counterattack, Instead, Scores 151

The disaster was turned into nothing, and the entire army counterattacked. Chen Hongguang passed to the center, Li Yichen passed to the right wing, and Cao Qiuting rushed up like a flying horse. Tau Que Dou saw that he had already caused trouble, so he hooked his foot. Ballard caught a glimpse of it and immediately awarded another penalty kick. Chen Jiaqiu sent the ball in with a bang, turning misfortune into fortune. Donghua really did not expect it. In Argyll's case, if this penalty kick had been scored, they would not have been penalized. This penalty kick, one in and one out, totaled two goals. Everyone knew that Argyll had lost. After that, although Argyll's momentum was overwhelming, many dangerous balls were blocked by the iron gate. The first half ended 2-0.

One Fell Swoop, Three Goals in a Row 152

Argyll lost two goals in a row. From the beginning of the second half, they continued to counterattack in an effort to retaliate. However, although the attack was fierce, it was still useless. Donghua then went deep into the enemy's territory, reaching the Scottish army's goal. Wan Xianghua crossed and Chen Hongguang headed the ball, which fell from high to low. The goalkeeper Henry and Si De jumped up to compete, but the ball was not caught and fell into the net at that moment, making it 3-0.

Endless Turmoil in Front of the Iron Gate 153

Argyll was in a situation of utter defeat and still continued to make persistent efforts, their courage commendable. Hai Shi received the ball and shot very urgently. The goalkeeper caught it but failed, dodging. The ball hit Wu Youliang's foot again, escaping danger. Then, Donghua was penalized for a foul in front of the goal. Hughes kicked the ball, which happened to be in Zhou Xianyan's hand. Taifei Xu shot at the goal in the chaos, thinking it would definitely go in, but it hit the goalpost and bounced back. Fortunately, Donghua, Hughes got a corner kick on the left, and Quitte headed the ball in, which was clear and spectacular, but the referee ruled that he had hit someone in the middle of the recording, so the goal was invalid.

A Desperate Gamble, Reclaiming One Goal 154

In the last five minutes, Argyll took a desperate gamble in the hope of reversing the situation of the entire army being wiped out, rushing towards Donghua's goal. Sure enough, Quitte took a long shot from 25 yards away. The iron gate thought it was a high ball that would go over the net and did not pounce, but unexpectedly it fell into the goal, making it 3-1 at the end of the game.

Research on Football Tactics (I) 159

Written in Response to the First Defeat of the Gunli Team in Batavia

After Li Junhuitang went to Batavia in the South Seas to do business, he never abandoned his football life. He and Cheng Lin also worked for the Chinese football team Gunli in that area. The team was very strong, unbeatable, and held the title of the local alliance leader. Unexpectedly, last week, they lost 0-2 to the Ali Feifei team. Li Jun felt that the unexpected defeat was due to the abnormality of luck, but felt that there was great value in researching tactics, so he wrote "Research on Football Tactics". Although it was published to seek future improvements for Gunli's failure, it is also worthy of reference for other football teams. The following is specially disclosed so that the Shanghai Chinese team and the domestic football community will pay attention to it (Editor).

Time flies so fast. It seems like a week has passed in an instant since Gunli suffered its first defeat this season. Originally, I wanted to write an article a few days ago, but I was a little busy with my recent appointment at the China Anbao Life Insurance Company and could not spare the time. I have delayed it until now before I can talk to you all. I hope everyone will not regard it as yesterday's news.

Gunli held the temporary alliance leader's fortress for only two weeks before it was destroyed by two shells from Ali Feifei and surrendered to others. In fact, what is there to talk about after a defeat? People will suspect that I am making excuses, relying on others, and shirking responsibility. But I have no such thoughts at all. I firmly believe that we were not unlucky that day, and I do not admit that the referee had any biased behavior, nor dare I say that the performance of our participants that day was completely abnormal, Off Form (I believe everyone has done their best, but the horse may not advance). If I say further that Ali Feifei won by luck, that is even more absurd. According to the situation and playing style that time, their victory was well deserved. To be honest, if Gunli's measures that day could have defeated Ali Feifei, I would not have been able to compliment them very much, because the strategies we adopted for responding to the enemy and attacking and defending were completely contrary to the truth. Even if the two teams played ten more games, if both sides still used the formation and tactics of that day, Gunli's hope of victory would probably only account for two or three out of ten. From this, it can be seen that the mystery and change of football are infinite. You cannot say that a strong team can definitely beat a weak team (everyone recognizes that Gunli is stronger), nor can you insist that a certain offensive and defensive method can succeed every time. Although the goddess of luck sometimes has a few latent controlling powers over victory and defeat in a football match (not a very common component), we must not completely rely on or complain about the goddess of luck. We must have a constant research, a "temporary change", "wisdom and common sense in the game", and "good methods and skills that can be adapted to the environment at any time". Only with these treasures can we often control the chances of winning. These treasures should be personal belongings that everyone in the team has. As soon as they are needed, they can be taken out immediately. Otherwise, it is really difficult for a large battlefield to cooperate. No matter how many talented people there are in your team, it is useless if they do not respond to each other, let alone that others are not completely powerless.

From here, let me first talk about the reasons for our frustration. The formation adopted by Ali Feifei that day is called the "Middle Road Blocking Defense Genre Blocking Defense". Their intention was only to prevent us from winning, and as for whether their forwards could build a career, they listened to the opportunity. They knew that I and my old partner A Dai Linjing were the most active and dangerous people, so they used three or four people to monitor them (very strict monitoring, even more severe than watching prisoners), in order to contain our front line. They believed that this kind of formation and strategy was very refined and wonderful and would definitely be effective (yes, in the end, they really relied on Gunli to break through the formation without defense and succeed). But in my opinion, that kind of formation is not a good one. The so-called sitting in a city will eventually lead to death. However, they were fortunate enough to encounter the current Gunli team, which had no ability to break this kind of formation. Otherwise, if a team that can use a scattered attack method, Odenupof Oenfense, they have no reason not to lose. I believe that their back often ignores the attacks on both wings, and only cares about retreating in the middle, which is no different from leading a wolf into the room, the next best policy (Fortunately, the wolves were not very fierce that day. If we had a pair of side generals like Ye Beihua and Cao Guicheng, carrying the ball all the way to the end line, and then throwing the ball high from above in front of the enemy's goal and doing it again and again, it would not be difficult to get things done and achieve good results. But that day, the centering skills of our side generals were very disappointing. They were either mistaken in time or mistaken in the standard, feeling tired back and forth, giving the enemy guards a good opportunity to create heroes. Secondly, the ball supply skills of the three central guards, Centering, also have a lot of room for improvement. The most obvious weakness is that after getting the ball, they cannot use wonderful passes to supply the forwards (although the ball is won wonderfully, the ball supply is not good, it is futile and time-consuming, and the chopping skills are still lacking. Feeding Cnop (chopping is a ball that is only slightly above people's heads. It is best to transmit it to your own forward when the enemy is trying to seize it in front of you. It is one of the most suitable kicking methods for the central guard.) Like that day, when you saw that the middle road was too tightly entangled, you should not still stubbornly stick to one hard road and make progress in the middle, causing blockage. You should carry the ball to a suitable place after getting the ball, or lure one of the enemy guards to seize it, and use the chopping method to transmit it to both wings and develop from the periphery to disrupt the enemy's formation. However, that day, the chopping-style kicking method and long pass, and the steps of the two wings were not often seen in the entire dike. Therefore, the enemy's suitable plan took the opportunity to be sold, and they still stationed a heavy army in the middle road regardless of other brothers. Although in fact there were more attacks and fewer defenses, because they could not find a way to lure the enemy to disperse, the opportunity for the forwards to shoot was reduced and they were unable to succeed, but were instead attacked by them twice. Therefore, according to the battle situation that day, to sum up, it is not so much that Ali Feifei's forwards won the ball, Tian Ning said that Ali Feifei's back won, and it is not so much that Ali Feifei overthrew Gunli, but rather that Gunli itself overthrew Gunli. The reasons for our failure are nothing more than the following: (1) The centering skills of both wings were not proper; (2) The supply of the ball in the center could not be changed according to the situation; (3) Since I and A Dai were seriously monitored, the team still often thought of giving the ball to the two of us, and no one outside of the two of us really had the ability to shoot; (4) Under the fierce attack, the back forgot its position, and after the enemy's forward got the ball, it took advantage of the emptiness to succeed.

Now, although things have passed, if we do not seek to cheer up after a failure, it is great cowardice. What's more, it is not too late to mend the fold after the sheep is lost. The future of the championship is unlimited. The materials of our team, Malenrial, are not inferior, and anyone is a good material that can be created. The general requirement is that the person himself is willing to carefully ponder, accept with humility, adopt and avoid shortcomings, and work hard. According to my observation, the teammates of Gunli are not a generation of stubborn stones that "can neither command nor be commanded". Everyone must know that if you want to enjoy a great name in everything, it cannot be achieved overnight. Great name and success cannot be brought with you from the womb. Although sometimes art can create heroes, a person "only can create himself" and must not be willing to be a coward who relies solely on luck or the times to patronize (To be continued)

Free Talk

Short Story

Stealing a Belt Buckle Leads to Execution (Part 2) 160

— Zhu Wen

The others, hearing this, seemed to think of their own affairs and slowly dispersed. Da Fa returned to his sleeping place and kicked San De hard out of irritation. San De, like a pig, did not wake up and just fell back asleep.

He then had another dream.

When he woke up from this strange dream, someone was kicking him violently. Thinking that they were the people who were going to arrest him, he jumped up suddenly, opened his eyes wide, and saw a black man in coarse cloth, holding a bamboo carrying pole. The man, caught off guard by Da Fa's sudden jump, was also startled and opened his eyes wide.

"Pig, are you crazy?... I'm going to do business, why are you still lying here?"

Da Fa saw a load of small green vegetables next to the carrying pole. He looked further and saw many large baskets and crates filled with goods, and several small stalls, the wooden frames of which were hung with pork and beef. Everyone was busy organizing their own baskets or stalls. He also saw San De wiping his face with a blue cloth coat, looking quite energetic.

"There was a shooting in the middle of the night to catch robbers. I ran to watch. I don't know if the robbers were caught, but someone died senselessly while they were changing locations."

"Don't let them mistake you for a robber," San De said coldly.

"I pushed you a few times, wanting to call you to go and see, but you slept like a pig. How could I wake you up?"

"It's a good thing I didn't wake up. If I had really been woken up by you, I would have broken your bones."

As he was saying this, San De had already put on his clothes and was about to leave when he felt a cold, wet sensation under his feet, which angered him. He looked down and saw a slow stream of water flowing over his feet. Looking back, he knew where the water came from. The man who had kicked Da Fa a couple of times had placed a large basket of vegetables next to a pipe. Clean water flowed from the pipe, and the water that washed over the vegetables flowed straight down the stone slab from under the basket, soaking San De's feet. He was about to shout in anger, but when he saw the good, clean water, he pulled Da Fa and walked over together. The vegetable seller turned a small device, and the water stopped flowing. Da Fa asked in surprise:

"What is this? This thing is really good."

"This is tap water."

The two of them washed their hands and faces. Their hands felt very refreshed, but their faces still didn't feel quite right. They couldn't put their faces directly under the pipe, so they joined their palms together, forming a large bowl, waited for it to fill with water, and then rubbed it on their faces. Then they drank a lot of water in the same way before walking away happily.

This street was now very different from yesterday. Now, both sides were piled high with vegetables. In some places, there were also small baskets selling snacks, with pieces of square cakes and triangular white rice cakes steaming with soft heat, as well as piles of cooked noodles. They stood for a while and saw several peddlers sitting by a long bench, paying a few copper coins for a bowl of noodles. The noodles were only seasoned with soy sauce and sesame oil, but they looked like a high-quality dish.

With no hope of buying anything from these stalls, they mingled with the crowd of shoppers. More and more women carrying small baskets slowly appeared, sniffing at the various goods like dogs. A chaotic mix of sounds, along with the fishy and meaty smells of various items, entered their ears and noses, and the various goods also attracted their eyes. There were tiny heads of small green vegetables, chicken greens, large eggplants, pods of edamame, and many other things that they had at home, things they had planted themselves. Now, everything seemed very precious, and they wished they could reach out and grab a handful, which would surely taste good even eaten raw.

San De and Da Fa both thought this. It would be great if they could steal such a handful. If the person saw them and made a fuss, they would just return it. But San De saw a well-dressed woman also buying vegetables in the crowd, so he thought that after these people bought good things, it would be much fairer to reach into their baskets to steal than to steal from the peddlers. Because Da Fa was thinking about his hometown that had been flooded, he stood blankly next to a tofu stall, not even seeing his companion carefully eyeing many small baskets.

Dream 161

— Han Xing

In this world, we have never seen a "perfect person." Therefore, whether you are poor or rich, whether you are a commoner or a great figure, whether you are a child or an old person, as long as you close your eyes and sleep soundly, you will dream.

According to Freud's analysis, dreams are the result of repressed subconscious desires taking over when a person's conscious mind is asleep and loses control. These desires, which are usually suppressed because they are longed for but cannot be satisfied, are disguised and acted out in various forms. From this, we can know that only dreams are truly free. When you are sound asleep, you can instantly become a millionaire, instantly become a high-ranking official, kiss the young man or woman you adore, or kill the enemies you hate. You can ride the wind and soar through the sky, or float on the water and bob on the sea.

In short, there are no laws, morals, customs, or any other restraints or restrictions here. Your consciousness can run wild like an untamed horse, and you can satisfy everything you hope for but cannot achieve.

A young boy or girl often has rosy dreams, a businessman often has dreams of getting rich, and a politician often has dreams of rising to prominence. However, many people often have nightmares, dreams of revenge, such as when a group of starving and freezing slaves stretch out their legs and lie haphazardly in a dark underground room after a day of fatigue. Can you know what kind of dreams they are having?

Only in dreams are we truly free, and we can be whatever we imagine. Therefore, smart people are often dreaming, sometimes even daydreaming. For example, smart people say that justice can eventually overcome power, or that puppets can eventually come to life. Even if this is just a "dream," children, can you be sure that it won't become a reality in the "future future"?

The True Face of a Man 162

— Ms. Wan Zhen

When a man is in the process of courtship, his words and actions are truly pitiful and laughable. When he prepares to see his beloved, he has to groom himself for a long time like a so-called young lady in her boudoir—shaving, applying cold cream, spraying hair water, combing his hair sleekly, polishing his leather shoes until they shine, and then changing into a brand new outfit, tugging and pulling to tie his tie properly. Finally, he inserts a beautiful little silk handkerchief into the small pocket on his chest. Then, shrugging his shoulders, twisting his neck, looking left and right, he strides out.

But as soon as he sees his beloved, he instantly transforms the lively, dashing, and complacent attitude he had on the way into nothingness. Now, he is as frightened and cautious as a subject seeing his king or a servant seeing his master, waiting for orders with his hands at his sides. When he speaks, he always puts on a smiling face, diligently compliments her, and does everything he can. If he sees his beloved looking unhappy, he hangs his head in despair as if he has committed a crime, unable to sit or stand still, unable to eat or sleep, completely at a loss. When he sees his beloved smile, he is as joyful and elated as a prisoner being pardoned or a dried-up fish being returned to water. In order to achieve the goal of being loved, he will say to his beloved in a pleading and sighing tone: "I don't pursue anything in the world. My only wish is to be your servant, your slave, forever. I want to live for you, die for you, I wish..." How pitiful and sweet-sounding it is!

After love is sought and the goal is achieved, he is still very gentle and docile during this period. He is extremely concerned and considerate about everything his beloved does. If his beloved wants him to go up the mountain, he will go up the mountain; if she wants him to go into the water, he will go into the water. If his beloved wants this, he will do this; if she wants that, he will do that. He is truly obedient and follows her every command. In short, at this time, he regards his beloved as a goddess, and her words as a sacred decree. He would not hesitate to go through fire and water or be crushed to pieces for her. Now he is married to her. At first, he naturally continues to show her attentiveness and win her favor, but as time goes on, things slowly start to change. He is no longer as flattering, complimentary, respectful, or loving as he used to be. He is no longer as careful and obedient as he used to be. He now gradually wants to control everything and dominate everything, putting on the air of a husband as if he were invincible! Sometimes, when he is unhappy, he will glare at his wife, roar, and scold her, always using his wife as a punching bag. If his wife tries to advise him on something, he will say: "What do you know? Don't interfere in my affairs!"

As things progress, it gets even worse. He gradually becomes tired of his beloved, and he has other pursuits. He simply can't stay at home. He is out all day long, and when he occasionally comes back, he doesn't have a good face for his wife. If his wife asks him a few more questions, he will shout at her, saying that she is infringing on his freedom and not allowing her to nag.

In short, at this time, he has completely revealed his true colors, no, he has completely revealed the true face of a man!

Who Says Chinese Education Isn't Widespread? 163

— Shi

Whoever says Chinese education isn't widespread is blind. Look, there are no fewer than forty or fifty universities and specialized schools across the country. Agriculture, engineering, commerce, mathematics, physics, chemistry, literature, law, medicine, education, art, physical education... whatever subjects are available in the East, the West, various countries, we don't lack a single one. As for middle schools, provincial, county, public, private, they are everywhere in the country. And they also have specialized departments such as agriculture, engineering, commerce, literature, and education, not lacking a single one. Furthermore, there are even more primary schools that are too numerous to count. There are affiliated ones, county-run ones, city-run ones, township-run ones... In short, everything is available.

As for the lower classes and the remote villages, it's not desolate either. There are plenty of old-fashioned Confucian scholars who failed to pass the imperial examinations in the previous dynasty, wearing old-fashioned glasses, holding stiff rulers, chasing after a group of naughty children with runny noses, implementing the authentic national essence education of "Confucius said" and "The Book of Odes."

Moreover, there's no need to even mention popular education. And we have immediate examples. For instance, on the walls of small alleys, you can always see slogans such as "No Urinating," "Damn You for Urinating," etc., for those lower-class people who urinate at will to see. Some even draw a large turtle. This method of propaganda using picture literacy not only shows that the person writing it has received an education, but also contains profound educational significance. Furthermore, beggars in Shanghai often display a large passage in English, the writing is neat, the prose is fluent, and a translation is attached. Think about it, scholars who are knowledgeable in both Chinese and Western learning are only beggars. Isn't our country's education too widespread?

Therefore, I say, whoever says Chinese education isn't widespread is blind.

The Lolo People of Yunnan (Part 1) 164

— Wang Yu

Here, I plan to introduce to you the aborigines living in Yunnan.

These aborigines are commonly called "Lolo" by the Han people.

Speaking of Lolo, there seems to be more than one kind. There are so-called Flowery Lolo, Han Lolo, and Water Lolo.

Han Lolo are probably named because they are mostly close to the Han people. I will introduce this type here. As for the other two types, because I have never been in contact with them, I know as little about their lives as you do. I can't even explain the meanings of the words "Flowery" in Flowery Lolo and "Water" in Water Lolo. Now, let me report what I know to you.

(1) Language and Writing

These people have their own language and writing, and this language can also be used in the border areas of Myanmar. I heard that it is not difficult to learn. I have seen many people who are often in contact with them speak fluent Lolo. Even I myself have learned the pronunciation of the ten numbers one to ten.

Their writing is horizontal like Western writing. I heard that they also have an alphabet; however, what they use for writing is not a writing brush or a fountain pen, but the petiole of a fern (pteridophyte) after the veins have been removed. Writing with it is like writing with a steel pen, but it is not as smooth and durable as a steel pen.

As for books, apart from many religious scriptures, there seem to be no other works. And these scriptures are all handwritten. (2) Religious Beliefs

In every temple, we can find a huge idol of Sakyamuni, so we can assume that they believe in Buddhism. Their temples are called "Burmese Temples." The architecture of these Burmese Temples is very grand. Living in the Burmese Temples are a "Grand Buddha and several or even dozens of young monks." The Grand Buddha is sometimes also called "Elder." After he dies, his position is inherited by the oldest of the young monks. This oldest of the young monks is also called the "Second Buddha" when the elder is not yet dead. The young monks are all Lolo children. Some are volunteers who want to be monks, some are sent to the Burmese Temple by their parents, and some are designated to be monks.

The Grand Buddha cannot marry. However, the young monks can "return to secular life" when they want to marry, which means leaving the Burmese Temple and regaining their status as ordinary people.

Usually, there is one Burmese Temple in one or several villages. The Grand Buddha and the young monks in the Burmese Temple do nothing but chant scriptures. What they wear and eat is provided by the people of this one or several villages.

The Grand Buddha in this Lolo group is like the pastor in Christianity in medieval Rome. He will use Buddhist spells to cure people's illnesses. Every newborn child must ask the Grand Buddha to bless him with longevity and give him a rope with many knots tied around his neck. This probably means that his soul is not allowed to leave his body. When a person passes away from this world, the Grand Buddha must also pray for his peace and happiness after death and surround his grave with a straw rope tied with many mysterious knots, which probably means to protect him and not allow anything else to invade him. The Lolo treat the Grand Buddha like a god. Even the Buddha's father and mother must kowtow to the Buddha. Regarding this matter, the general explanation is that his parents do not respect him, but respect his "yellow robe." The so-called yellow robe is the clothing of the Grand Buddha and the young monks. This is completely different from ordinary clothes. They wrap a piece of yellow cloth around their lower body as trousers, and wrap a larger piece of yellow cloth around their upper body like women in the city use scarves as clothes. However, these two pieces of yellow cloth are by no means whole pieces, but are made of several square pieces of cloth arranged in a certain way.

Just as Christians go to church every Sunday to "attend mass," the Lolo people also go to the Burmese Temple on certain days to "drip water."

Long Creative Work

Crossroads of the Times and Love 12 165

— Zhang Ziping

Haiquan was already somewhat tired of student life, especially science studies. Moreover, his age had exceeded twenty, so he couldn't avoid suffering from a kind of youth disease prevalent among young people: boredom. Originally, this kind of adolescent boredom was very easy to cure, as long as the right medicine was prescribed. What medicine? That is, to liberate their sexual and economic oppression. But before Chinese society is transformed, it is not easy for young people to be liberated from this boredom. Young people who are oppressed naturally have many complaints. From complaints to lamentations, it eventually manifests as a distorted form of literature, dominating the entire literary scene in China. Although Haiquan aspired to study science, he sometimes felt that there was no hope for the future, so he couldn't help but feel pessimistic. At the same time, like ordinary young people, he was subjected to the aforementioned oppression, and lived in boredom all the time. Therefore, he would sometimes voice a few complaints, lament his own life, and express it in the form of poetry or prose. Tang Yaoxing knew that he also liked to doodle and write, so he came to persuade him to join the literary society they had organized.

"Are you willing to be our member?"

Tang Yaoxing's attitude was very sincere. This could be seen intuitively. Haiquan suddenly felt that his attitude was admirable, but he was still hesitant.

"Me?..."

He tilted his head as if he was thinking deeply, as if it was very difficult to make a decision.

"Do you have any doubts?"

"I don't have any doubts. But I want to meet Mr. Chen Huamin first and ask him about his literary views. He can't take Art for Art's sake as his position like we do, right?"

"Of course not. He is someone with literary views. What you said is right. I'll make an appointment with him first and have you meet. But you must be absolutely secret! Don't tell any classmates, because there are too many literary groups in the school now, mutually slandering and undermining each other..."

"Then I understand..."

As Haiquan said this, he suddenly went from literary arts to thinking about the students in the literature department, and from the students in the literature department to thinking about Miss Zhuo he saw this morning.

"...Are you recruiting female members?"

"Not for the time being. Chinese women don't have much power yet."

"What do you think of Zhuo Shuhua in the literature department?"

After Haiquan said this, he felt a little embarrassed.

"You think she's pretty, don't you? Ha, ha!"

"Nonsense!"

"She's a useless person!"

Tang Yaoxing used these five words in a stern tone to completely dismiss Miss Zhuo.

"Why? As long as she can write articles, that's enough. I heard that her poetry is quite good."

"The literary arts that are needed today are not just literary arts of blood and tears. The most important condition is the condition of strength..."

Yaoxing seemed to be saying this very enthusiastically.

"...Do you think Miss Zhuo is someone who can write literary arts of strength? She's just wiggling around in her high-heeled dancing shoes..."

Economic Special Issue Published every Monday, Issue 2

Commodity Production Reduction and Global Economic Trends 166

— Wang Yu-huan

Since the Wall Street Stock Exchange in the United States staged a chaotic drama in 1929, the economic situation in the United States has plummeted, becoming unmanageable, and the phenomenon of recession has spread throughout the world. To this day, it has gone through a long period of more than two and a half years of decline, and the depth of the scene is unprecedented. According to the economic situation index listed in The Analist magazine, the extent of the economic panic in the United States reached a peak of 110.1% in May 1929, but suddenly dropped to 92.1% in December. Since then, it has gradually declined to 74.0% in August 1931, which has gradually revealed the acute form of panic. Moreover, with the general decline in prices, such as cotton, in August 1931, it had fallen from 12 cents per pound the year before to 6 cents, and wheat had fallen from 85 cents to 50 cents. The number of bank failures in the United States has reached as many as 1,210 by September of this year.

Overproduction and increased unemployment are the most important reasons for the current economic downturn in the world. In order to protect their own industries and increase national financial income, countries are competing to engage in tariff wars, building high tariff barriers in an attempt to drive out foreign economic forces and indirectly enrich national financial income. Although this kind of non-violent war behavior is enough to alleviate the economic recession temporarily, it is ultimately not a correct plan to abandon the fundamentals and pursue the superficial.

The reason why the original economic panic occurred is that the world economy has suddenly lost its balance today, which has led to it. Therefore, in addition to the protective tariff policy, the so-called controlled economy has emerged at the same time, and countries have adopted it as an important economic policy. The implementation methods of controlled economy do not go beyond two paths: one is to manage exchange rates, and the other is to manage trade. The former lies in adjusting the currency of the country to prevent the outflow of cash abroad, and the latter lies in restricting unnecessary foreign imports in order to improve international lending. These two are implemented simultaneously in some countries, and only one is limited in others. In short, their goal is to try to alleviate economic panic and return to the road of prosperity.

Recently, countries have also taken measures to reduce production in order to save the economic downturn. The most notable example is Cuban sugar, whose production volume in the 1929-30 year was 4,671,000 tons. It is said that from the coming year, it will be reduced to 2 million tons. Also, Java sugar was 2,903,000 tons in 1929-30, and it will also be reduced to 1,350,000 tons in the coming year.

Wheat is also one of the world's important commodities. In recent years, the market price has been greatly affected due to the good harvest and excessive supply. Recently, various places have risen up to find ways to implement production reduction. In the United States, the production volume this year and the remaining amount of 320 million bushels from last year are combined, which is 990 million bushels. In the future, the domestic consumption volume will need 750 million bushels, and the export volume will be 80 million bushels. As a result, the remaining amount for the next year will be 160 million bushels, which is half the state of last year. In Canada, according to the latest forecast, the harvest will be reduced by 27 million bushels this year. According to the telegraph on November 15 this year, Australian wheat will be reduced by about 27 million bushels. Romania's net export volume this year is expected to decrease by 10 million bushels. Also, Soviet Russia is expected to reduce production by 740 million bushels this year.

Also, according to the recent announcement by the U.S. Department of Agriculture and Commerce, this year's cotton production will be the lowest in the past nine years. The number of acres planted with cotton in the United States has been sharply reduced, and there are even more cotton fields suspended in Egypt. It was predetermined to reduce cotton harvest by 33%. Although the cotton harvest in Brazil, Mexico, and Lower India is estimated to reach 4.2 million bales, an increase of 800,000 bales compared with the previous year, and the cotton production in China and Persia has also increased, it is estimated that the world's production volume is only 23.4 million bales. Among them, the harvest in the United States will be between 11 million and 12 million bales. It is found that in 1923, the world's cotton harvest was 19.125 million bales, and it suddenly increased to 23.825 million bales the following year. Since then, the surplus has accumulated day by day, and cotton prices have fallen sharply. Now it is the first sharp reduction in the past nine years.

Sugar, wheat, and cotton are in the most important position in the world's commodities. The quantity of their annual production and consumption is enough to greatly affect the future of the world economy. According to the above-mentioned circumstances, the major sugar-producing countries such as Cuba and Java, and the wheat and cotton-producing countries such as the United States and Australia, can implement production reduction plans, which is helpful to the future of the world economy and is not shallow. If we can continue to advance in this direction in the future, we can believe that the future of the world's production undertakings will gradually be able to get rid of the state of oversupply and sluggish demand, and return to the path of balance. The results obtained are certainly better than the protective tariff policy that seeks the welfare of one's own country. From this, we can know that in today's economic world that is trapped in the abyss of recession and cannot be revitalized, if we want to seek true relief, we must rely on mutual cooperation and the spirit of sincerity to work hard. Otherwise, if we allow this to continue, the economic policies of using neighboring countries as a dumping ground will see countries competing to follow suit, and the total collapse of the world economy will inevitably be imminent.

World Cotton Production and Sales 167

— Yin

Since the beginning of this century, the past cotton season (up to the end of July this year) has been the worst, and cotton producers will never forget it. The average price of American cotton (American Upland) from 1931 to 1932 was US$0.0589 per pound, compared with US$0.174 per pound from 1929 to 1930, and US$0.076 per pound from 1899 to 1900, which was known as a low price. The combination of these two reasons caused this tragic situation to occur. The world panic is indeed a powerful reduction in the needs of textile manufacturers. Except for 1925-26 and 1926-27, the production volume from 1931 to 1932 was more than any year. In the United States, Egypt, and other places, even after government intervention to prevent the downward trend of market prices, it was of no use. On the contrary, the demand showed very little for cheap raw materials. The following table is a statistic of the world's cotton supply, mill consumption, and market prices in recent years.

At that time, the production and import volume of the United States was superior to the production of foreign countries. However, in recent years, the demand for Egyptian cotton has not changed much.

In addition, the governments of the United States and Egypt, in order to oppose the policy of cotton storage exceeding the market, have reduced the planted acreage to remedy it. In addition to increasing demand or poor harvest, this is to solve the excess supply and the unprofitable reduction of one-tenth. Egypt will reduce it by about 20%. The cotton stored in the United States is still higher than before until the end of this season. Therefore, the first public estimate of cotton production was published, which caused the cotton price, which had not yet fallen completely, to rise suddenly. Until October, the public estimate of cotton production was about 11.425 million bales, while in 1932-1933, the actual production was 17.096 million bales. As for the Egyptian cotton production volume, it is estimated to decrease from 1.288 million bales to 869,000 bales compared to last year's harvest. If the cotton consumption rate of last year can still be maintained as before in this year, until the current season, the cotton stored in the United States and Egypt can still be reduced in quantity. Although the world's supply and possible consumption cannot be estimated, it seems impossible for the cotton price to fall to the low price found at the beginning of the year. However, in the near future, unless the planted acreage in the United States and other places is reduced again, and then other goods cause the price of a large amount of stored cotton to be firmly fixed and increase, the cotton market situation is fundamentally different from wool. The amount of wool collected has already met the needs of the market, and there is no excessive accumulation of cotton yarn in the hands of producers. Before cotton production is more favorable to cotton producers, cotton producers will have a major burden due to the supply restricted by human power.

Soviet Russia's Foreign Trade in the Decline of World Commerce 168

— Jianchu

The Soviet Russia's foreign trade is exclusively operated by the government. The export of goods is continuous. However, its purpose is not commercial competition, but to absorb foreign currency to pay for the value of planned imports. The domestic market often feels insufficient, but the export volume has never declined, which is actually because the power of foreign trade is in the hands of the government. The goods imported each year are based on the Five-Year Plan, rather than good and urgently needed goods, and are mainly used to assist production, especially industry and construction. Daily necessities are the most lacking, and imports are almost extinct. The point of view of a country with state-run trade is very different from that of other countries. The prices in Soviet Russia are all determined by the government, standing tall and independent, and not affected by the world market. Price fluctuations are purely determined by domestic reasons, and have little to do with the trend of world prices. The currency value of Soviet Russia is also designated by the government, and there is no fear of momentary changes. At this time of panic and anger, when the world is agitated, if we want to understand the foreign trade of Soviet Russia, we must first know the above-mentioned characteristics.

The world economic panic is in full swing, and prices have fallen miserably, falling thousands of miles, and the impact on Soviet Russia seems to be very subtle. Because in recent years, prices in Soviet Russia have risen, and the trend of agricultural products has been particularly sharp. The prices in Soviet Russia are so-called cooperative prices, which are stipulated by the authorities, and the number of sales is also limited, and they are only sold to people who enjoy the right to purchase the item. This kind of price has changed little in 1931, while the price in the free market has soared and soared. The difference between the cooperative price and the self-price is huge, which is enough to see the urgency and urgency of the Soviet Russian people. The government's supply of daily necessities is insufficient, so they turn to merchants to buy them. The prices are slightly higher, but they are not counted. Therefore, in 1931, due to the lack of necessities, the increase in retail prices was particularly rapid, and the world prices were trying to pour out, so it seemed impossible to export necessities. However, judging from the actual situation, it is very different. Key products that are urgently needed in the domestic market are continuously exported, and the prices are extremely low and the losses are huge, because the government of Soviet Russia pays for the value of imports. Kaganovch, the spokesman of the Soviet Russian government, also said because he could not overcome the supply of consumers, "We have built major factories and must continue. Therefore, our export trade will never let go." This is enough to explain the attitude of Soviet Russia. At this time of world unease, trade in various countries is sluggish, but in 1931, Soviet Russia's export trade has greatly increased. This is also because the government is working hard to promote it, and both cost and people's livelihood are not counted, so there is this畸 形development.

The situation of Soviet Russia's foreign trade in 1931 and the first half of 1932 is roughly as follows:

Therefore, the impact of the world panic in 1931 on Soviet Russia's foreign trade was the miserable fall in the value of export goods, while the export volume increased slightly. As for its preferential treatment of import trade and cheap prices, although many years of old debts have not been paid off, it can still obtain new loans to support it, which is deeply benefited.

In the first half of 1932, the value of export goods decreased sharply, and the import business also suffered setbacks. Although the process of domestic industrialization cannot be delayed, due to the impact of the world recession, it has to slow down its pace slightly. Therefore, in 1932, the pressure of the world panic was far greater than in 1931, and Soviet Russia could not stand aloof from the world, but had to share its fate with various countries and tighten its foreign trade. The difficulties in the domestic economy are becoming more and more serious, the lack of agricultural products, and the failure to implement industrial plans have made the Soviet Russian authorities exhausted. Therefore, this year's foreign trade in Soviet Russia will inevitably have a large decrease.

A Brief Discussion on Modern Currency (1) 169

— Translated by Ke

The issue of currency has been extremely complex since ancient times, and its impact is greatly related to people's livelihoods and national economy. Therefore, many intelligent people have paid close attention to it, and there are also many related works. The economies of various countries are showing signs of decline, and the international financial hub has also lost its function. Various currency problems have emerged like bamboo shoots after rain, all at once. The complexity of their roots and the breadth of their involvement are truly enough to make wise people stammer and capable people withdraw their hands. However, the world's currency problems cannot remain unresolved for long, or it will leave endless troubles. Therefore, researchers have emerged one after another, producing great works and short chapters, offering various opinions. Some present profound principles, while others discuss partial problems. The lower ones even engage in useless propaganda for their own interests. It is rare to find someone who can point out the essence of the principles and problems with a fair attitude and simple language so that everyone can understand. This spring, Mr. D.B. Woodward and Mr. Marc A. Rose published the book "A Brief Discussion on Modern Currency." Although its content has no unique insights, it discusses matters based on facts, without preconceived notions, and is comprehensive and detailed. Reading it does not cause any obstacles. Therefore, we specially asked Mr. Ke to translate and publish it in installments in this publication for the study of our countrymen. - Editor's note

Chapter 1: The Origin of Currency

To understand the origin of currency, we must first clarify its definition. Now, let us examine Webster's Dictionary, which defines the word "currency" as any object that is used as a medium of exchange and also serves as a standard of value is currency. Therefore, gold, silver, and round coins are currency. Even fur, silk, shells, and salt, if used as a medium of exchange and a standard of value, are also currency. Moreover, in fact, these things have all been used as currency by various primitive peoples. For example, otter skins were still used as currency and circulated in the Americas in the 18th century.

It is impossible to determine when and where the use of currency first began. It is said that coins first circulated in Egypt and Lydia. According to recent research, Lydia may have come first. However, the use of currency far predates the invention of coins, so the true picture of its initial circulation cannot be known.

However, one thing is certain: the invention of currency was not the sole act of any one nation. All nations in the world gradually evolved from barbaric life to a period of intellectual development. Human affairs became more complex, desires increased, the use of goods became more widespread, and transactions became laborious. Therefore, they felt the importance of a medium of exchange and a standard of prices, and thus invented and used currency. Therefore, the use of currency became a universal trend. No one nation can claim the sole credit for its invention, just as the invention and development of writing were achieved separately by various nations.

Although we cannot know the exact place and time of the origin of currency, we can generally understand its trend of evolution. Now, let us first look at the main facts of the matter, so that we can learn from the past and avoid being clueless when discussing current currency problems.

Humanity's basic needs are clothing, food, and shelter. People can compete with nature using their own intelligence and physical strength, and obtain what they need from nature's embrace to satisfy their desires. However, under this mode of production, the results are often meager and insufficient for use. If they can focus their energy on one thing, the results will be far better than when dividing their attention among various things. However, the establishment of this specialization must first require trade. In an economic life where division of labor and trade coexist, a person can exchange their specialized products with others to obtain other necessities to meet their living needs. The simplest form of this kind of transaction is the direct form of bartering, which is called direct exchange. However, direct exchange can only be carried out in the simplest societies. In complex societies, the number of traders is large, and the goods traded are also numerous. At this point, direct exchange reaches its limit. If we want to promote this matter to benefit people's lives, we must invent a medium that can exchange any goods and is desired by everyone. With this thing, everyone can specialize in one industry, exchange the results of their work for this thing that the public desires, and then use this thing to exchange for all the necessities of life they need. In this situation, the transaction changes from direct to indirect.

This universal commodity used as a medium of exchange is currency. Any commodity can be used as currency. In fact, this is exactly the case. In ancient China, shells, silk, and deer skins were used. The people of Aztec used coconuts. The early colonists of America used tobacco. Some Indian tribes used coal, and added carvings to enhance its beauty.

Several kinds of goods are particularly desired because of their quality, such as bread and salt. A person owns an axe and exchanges it for salt and stores it. At the beginning of the transaction, he may not need salt, but he sees that this salt can be exchanged for any other thing he needs in the future, so he develops a need for it and wants to exchange for it and treasure it. Therefore, the reason why salt is desired is not only because it can be used for food, but also because it can be exchanged for any other kind of goods at any time. In this case, salt is currency. This is also true for other things. These goods that become currency all have considerable characteristics: (1) Their quantity must be relatively small, but not too scarce. (2) Their body must be divisible for transactions of various amounts. (3) Their body must be light and easy to carry, so that they can be transported without loss. (4) Their quality must be solid, durable, and not easily damaged. Salt, rice, shells, and silk all have these qualities. This standard is perfectly in line with the conditions for modern ideal currency, which shows the meticulousness of the ancients' thinking.

Later, the types of currency used in trade gradually decreased, and the selection of currency was no longer a matter of thought and consciousness. The selection came from a gradual process of trial and error, using the most popular things as currency. During this period, a new important quality of currency appeared, that is, it must be able to satisfy people's desire for decoration. Anything that can be used for decoration is the best medium of exchange. Treasures are like currency, durable, rare, and of high value, but not too heavy, so they are often used as currency. Piles of ornaments, bracelets, and other objects are also like this, because they have all been widely used as currency.

After currency came into circulation, prices followed. When there was no currency, the so-called price was only the quantity of one thing used to exchange for another. After the use of currency replaced the fact of direct exchange, the price of goods began to be measured in currency. Therefore, economists often say that currency is a medium of exchange and a standard of prices. In addition to this, currency has another function, which is that it can be used as a store of value. After having currency, we no longer need to accumulate and store all our things, and then sell them to exchange for what we need. We can first sell all our things, exchange them for money to store, and then use this money to buy anything we need.

As transactions become more frequent, trade develops. However, the handling of trade is not necessarily completed at one time. Sometimes, due to various reasons, the payment of prices is always done later. Therefore, it is necessary to first stipulate what will be used to pay this price at that time, and what the quantity and quality will be. All these points can be well hidden by currency. Therefore, currency has a fourth use, that is, it can be used as a standard for deferred payments.

In short, since the invention of currency, the division of labor has become possible. People can specialize in one industry to develop specialized and advanced skills, which is the forerunner of higher industry in the future. People can also measure the price of their own products in currency to compare them with other things and determine the standard of exchange. They can also accumulate currency and exchange it for anything they need anytime and anywhere. In addition, they can use it for deferred payments and income to facilitate the conduct of business. In short, after having currency, people can create today's great business activities and economic civilization. (To be continued)

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking Points

Talking About Time 170

— I

With nothing to talk about, let's talk about time.

Many people say that Chinese people are not punctual. This is a big mistake. Chinese people value time. There are famous sayings throughout the ages to prove it. Dayu cherished every inch of time, and Tao Kan cherished every minute.

For example, if a certain group or expert meeting invites you to participate, and the time is set for 1:00 PM, then you should at least wait at home until 1:30 PM before putting on your Zhongshan suit and setting off. Upon entering the meeting place, you take off your hat, hand it to the attendant, and then shake hands with everyone and say hello. Finally, you slowly say, "I just went to visit a certain important party and state figure and talked about many major plans to save the country. I'm really too busy..." Thus, many comrades present will secretly marvel and respect you. This happens once or twice, and then your value will increase a hundredfold in an invisible way, because only important people are too busy with their time.

As for who invites you to drink, you can be at least two hours late, because if you go on time, the host's attendant will suspect that you haven't eaten for three days. Therefore, those who are well-versed in the ways of the world often deliberately arrive late, and it is best to leave after eating one or two dishes, preferring to go back and eat rice with boiled water, so as not to offend good manners.

Looking at it this way, there is a reason why Chinese people are not punctual. Can we still insult them arbitrarily like foreigners?

Time is something that circulates endlessly. If today is over, there is still tomorrow. Therefore, things that cannot be done today can be left for tomorrow. Things that you don't want to do today can be thought of later. Human energy is limited, so why should people be so diligent? Therefore, foreigners take time too seriously and exhaust their energy, which is inevitably foolish.

As for playing with time, it is the special skill of our compatriots, which cannot be denied. For example, when the Japanese army occupied the Northeast, we did not have to immediately send troops to save the country. We could take our time to appeal to the League of Nations, and we could take a hundred steps back and resist for a long time. The so-called "long time" of course means to continue indefinitely. If the Japanese army occupies Shanghai again today, we can wait until tomorrow to retreat to Tongguan along with the official seals. If they occupy Luoyang tomorrow, then we can retreat to the vast Gobi Desert of Outer Mongolia the day after tomorrow.

Sino-Japanese disputes can certainly wait for the League of Nations to resolve. As for the League of Nations wanting to divide China, then we can set up a water and land Taoist temple and piously pray to Heaven, waiting for the Jade Emperor to uphold justice.

Tomorrow, and tomorrow, and tomorrow, how much more of tomorrow is there? Life is not full of a hundred years, why not delay a little longer? This is my conclusion.

Feelings on Hearing of General Su Bingwen's Retreat 171
