The Hu Jia flute plays a mournful tune, the fate of the country hangs by a thread. Sighing that the chase for power continues in Sichuan and Guizhou, I feel alienated from the fields of the divine land.

It is difficult to support a tall building with a single pillar. What are the generals of the Central Plains doing? The isolated army is cut off and suffers destruction. Who else can save the country from disaster?

With the ambition to swallow rivers and mountains and save the world from difficulties, he endured the pain of retreating and secretly shed tears. If not for the general's courage to frighten the enemy, the Hu cavalry would have already crossed the Yuguan Pass.

Do not judge heroes by success or failure. How can loyal blood and a loyal heart be obscured? Yue Fei was loyal, and Qin Hui was a traitor. Praise and blame are the same in ancient and modern times.

Science

Method of Manufacturing Saccharin 172

— Erming

Ordinary crude sugar obtained from sugarcane or beets often contains ash and invert sugar. Therefore, it is often refined with bone char to obtain refined sugar. Refined sugar is white in color, and its quality is better than that of sugar made from sugarcane or beets. Therefore, I will briefly describe its manufacturing method.

Grade of Raw Sugar The grade of raw sugar, that is, crude sugar, depends on its color and the content of water, sucrose, glucose, and inorganic matter. The lighter the color, the more bone char can be saved during refining. The more glucose and inorganic matter it contains, the lower the yield of refined sugar. The yield of refined sugar is the percentage of sucrose calculated from the rotation, minus five times the percentage of inorganic matter (ash) and one times the percentage of glucose (the yield can be arbitrarily specified, for example, in Germany, the yield of beet sugar is defined as the percentage of sucrose minus five times the percentage of invert sugar). Ordinary crude sugar with a yield of 95% or more is excellent raw material. Recently, the use of preparatory treatment methods has been able to increase the grade of inferior sugar and make it suitable for the manufacture of refined sugar. The crystallization of raw sugar should be uniform, and it is best not to contain fine particles. Also, the amount of molasses attached should be as little as possible.

Sugar with wet properties often contains some invert sugar. Therefore, if beet sugar that does not contain any invert sugar is used as raw material to manufacture this kind of granulated sugar, it is usually mixed with an appropriate amount of cane sugar. Also, beet sugar is mostly alkaline, while cane sugar is mostly acidic. Therefore, when manufacturing refined sugar, they are also mixed in appropriate amounts to neutralize each other. In short, the blending of raw sugar is one of the most important projects in sugar manufacturing.

Preparatory Treatment Method of Raw Sugar Raw sugar is often subjected to preparatory treatment by mechanical methods to remove most of the impurities. In this method, thick sugar water is mixed into the raw sugar, and then a centrifugal machine is used to separate the molasses. At this time, auxiliary work such as spraying cold water or thick sugar water is often applied. However, there are also those who blow steam into the center of the centrifugal machine. In this way, the separation is more complete.

I Admire Your Great Name and Dare Not Accept Your Teachings. Lu Wan E 173

Page 18

Dissolution and Cleaning After the raw sugar has been treated with the preparatory method, it is placed in a dissolving pot to dissolve it. The pot is a square, open-ended iron cylinder with various diameters and a depth of about four to five feet, which can hold a solution containing three to ten tons of sugar. There is a false bottom in the center, and four steam spiral tubes are installed under the false bottom. Water is injected into the pot so that it submerges the steam tubes, and then steam is passed through it, adding an appropriate amount of heat. Next, water and sugar are added above the false bottom, and a rotating stirrer is installed under the false bottom to promote the dissolution of the sugar. Also, at the intersection of its right side and another room, there is a wire mesh made of brass. The dissolved sugar liquid flows out through this to remove large impurities and prevent them from going to the filter. The obtained sugar liquid is then filtered, or slightly cleaned in the dissolving pot or other cleaning device, and then filtered through a metal wire mesh to remove some of the impurities. Then it is filtered with a filter. Lime is mostly used as a cleaning agent, or a certain amount of phosphoric acid is added at the same time. In addition, there are also those who use aluminum sulfate and lime.

Decolorization The sugar liquid that has been filtered still has some color, so it must be passed through a bone char filter to decolorize it. The bone char filter is a large cylinder filled with bone char. Because bone char has a special absorption effect, it can remove the color quality. The device is made of cast iron or wrought iron and varies in size, such as 10 feet in diameter and 20 feet in height as an example. Bone char is loaded into the bone char filter from the upper opening and stacked on the cloth laid on the false bottom. Warm sugar liquid is pressed in through the pipe, passes through the bone char layer, and overflows into a receiver. After being tightly closed and placed for thirty or twenty hours, it is then allowed to flow out. When the decolorization power of the bone char decreases, warm water is sent in to fully wash it. The obtained dilute washing liquid can be used to dissolve raw sugar, or evaporated to make inferior sugar. The damp bone char is taken out from the opening on the lower side and appropriately heated. It can still be used repeatedly. This operation is called the regeneration of bone char.

Evaporation The sugar liquid that has been decolorized is then evaporated and concentrated. The commonly used method is vacuum evaporation, that is, evaporating the sugar liquid under low pressure. Using this method can make the sugar liquid boil and evaporate at around 50 degrees Celsius, so there is no danger of overheating, and it will not cause the conversion of sucrose. In addition, evaporation is rapid and steam consumption is minimal, which is very beneficial. Especially if several vacuum evaporators are connected, the steam generated by the first evaporator is used to heat the sugar liquid in the second evaporator, and the steam it generates is used to evaporate the sugar liquid in the third evaporator. This device is more economical. This type of device is called a multi-effect evaporation device, so it is the most widely used today.

Sugar Boiling and Crystallization The sugar liquid after evaporation still contains a large amount of water, so it must be evaporated and concentrated to make its water content only about 10%. This is called the sugar boiling method. After the sugar boiling method is performed, the crystallization method is performed. In modern large factories, these two operations are performed in a vacuum crystallizer. The vacuum crystallizer is a low cylinder made of cast iron, with several sections of steam spiral tubes inside to heat the sugar liquid. First, the pump is operated to reduce the pressure in the device, and then thick sugar liquid is injected until it completely covers the lowest section of the spiral tube. Then, steam is passed into the spiral tube, and the sugar liquid is gradually added. As it increases, steam is also passed through the serpentine tube at the top. When the sugar liquid reaches an appropriate concentration, new sugar liquid is quickly added, or the vacuum degree is increased, and the supply of steam is limited to slightly lower the temperature of the sugar liquid inside. As a result, fine crystal nuclei are generated in the sugar liquid. These are the seeds of crystalline sugar. More thick sugar liquid is added, and steam is passed through to continue boiling the sugar so that the crystals grow. When the crystals are full, the injection of sugar liquid and the passage of steam are stopped, and the bottom of the device is opened to take out the crystalline sugar paste.

Centrifugation The cooled crystalline sugar paste is crystalline granulated sugar attached with mother liquor (ie, molasses), so it must be separated. This is called the centrifugation method. Centrifugal machines are often used for centrifugation. First, the centrifugal machine is slowly rotated, and the crystalline sugar paste is added behind the screen. Then, it is rotated at a speed of about one thousand to one thousand five hundred times per minute, and the molasses passes through the screen holes to the outer cylinder. The refined sugar remains on the inner surface of the screen. If you want to make it more pure white, you can wash it with water containing a small amount of ultramarine during centrifugation.

Drying The refined sugar after centrifugation can be spread on the floor to cool and dry. If you want to get a sufficiently dry product, you can dry it in the sun or use a dryer.

Released from Prison 174

— Return I

At this time, it was after dusk, on this road known for its remoteness, the pale green streetlights were shining. Only the fallen leaves from the trees on both sides of the road, blown down by the west wind, occasionally rustled on the ground due to the breeze, breaking the deathly silence.

A thief who had just been released from prison today seemed to feel that he had no face to show to people of his kind, because he himself had lost his morality, and he knew that he had lost this morality. Also, he had no home to return to, and wanted to leave the crowd, but in the end he could not escape this world, so he came to this remote road to breathe a few breaths of air comfortably.

Three months ago, when his old mother was dangerously ill, he committed theft and was arrested by the patrol officers of the public security office and detained in prison. Although he has now served his sentence and been released from prison, he is still an unemployed person with no work to do and no place to eat. However, he now has no place to live. The tall houses, built on this land owned by mankind, although there are many, have never taken in people without money to live in.

He is still young, but his bleak complexion seems to indicate that he has deteriorated to the extreme. Outside his tattered cloth robe, he wore a straw rope, shrugged his shoulders, held a crude wooden stick that he had picked up from somewhere, and walked listlessly on this remote road.

A child walked towards him, singing a tuneless song and skipping, looking as if he was very happy. At a time when his mood was particularly bad, he was even a little jealous of other people's happiness, glared at the child, and caught sight of the streetlight shining on the child's slightly waving hand, on which a gold ring as thin as a thread was worn on the middle finger. He immediately began to calculate his life for tomorrow.

"Isn't this a great opportunity!" His heart was urging him.

"Although this thing is small, it is still worth a few dollars!" After thinking this, he calmly stopped the child's path.

"Why don't you let me go?"

"Take off this gold ring and give it to me!" He suddenly turned into a ferocious demon, and shouted at the child in a stern voice.

"This... this is my... thing!" The child was a little scared.

"You dare to be rude, you dare to disobey! You are just a weak child."

He grabbed the child and forcibly snatched the gold ring from the child's finger. As soon as he let go, the frightened child turned around and ran back crying.

He listened to the child's crying gradually fading away, and stood still next to the utility pole under the streetlight, staring at the gold ring in his palm in a daze, illuminated by the light. He was really a little proud to see this dazzling golden luster.

Suddenly, he shuddered and felt something, and chased after him, because his conscience suddenly developed and he regretted it.

He was very embarrassed; he ran a lot of roads forward, but besides himself, he didn't see a second person. Where could he find this child to return this gold ring? He had to shout loudly:

"Little boy! I'm playing with you, come here!"

He shouted like this several times, but there was no response, and he couldn't help but cover his face and cry bitterly. This was probably the first sad thing he had encountered in his life. But he continued to look for him, and saw a figure moving in front of him. He immediately ran up to see, but it was a little beggar of the same class as him.

"I have something to give you." He hurriedly said to the little beggar, and as he spoke, he stuffed the gold ring into the little beggar's hand. The little beggar, frightened as he had been when the child had been robbed of the gold ring, turned around and ran away.

Foreign Business 175

— Duan Rui

Last Saturday afternoon, taking advantage of the fact that there were no classes at school, I went to the XX Temple with three colleagues, including Ms. S, for a stroll and recreation. As soon as we entered the temple, we saw a group of devout men and women burning incense and lighting candles, their sincerity and piety indescribable, especially our female compatriots. After turning to the back of the temple, we suddenly saw three Westerners, accompanied by a translator, visiting the incense table. A leader knelt in front of the table and bowed his head three times, and then took a bamboo container of fortune sticks from the temple keeper, muttering and shaking the container. Then, he took out a stick, number twenty-four, marked "Bad Luck." The translator, seeing this, immediately went to the temple keeper and asked him to exchange it for a more favorable "Moderate Luck" yellow slip. The translator then explained the slip in detail. Listening closely, I learned that what they were praying about was the political turmoil in their country. After hearing the translation, they showed a happy expression and wanted to leave. The translator told them that they had to pay for the incense. They gave three foreign banknotes, and the temple keeper thanked them repeatedly after receiving them. According to the temple keeper, he had been in the temple for decades and this was the first time he had done foreign business. According to the reporter, although this matter is small, it is enough to show the concern of people from that country about national affairs.

Correspondence from Store Employees

Proposed Answer to Mr. Zhou Liangji's Fifth Question 176

"Original Question" "Standing in the position of a shop employee, worker, or apprentice, how can one fulfill the obligations of a citizen of the Republic of China and engage in the work of resisting Japan and saving the nation?"

"Proposed Answer" Generally, shop employees, workers, or apprentices are all employed by others. Besides being loyal to their duties, any other actions are enough to incur the jealousy of managers and supervisors. Although they may not be able to do anything to you for engaging in the work of resisting Japan and saving the nation, they often easily use other issues as pretexts to subject you to very harsh punishments. The question raised by Mr. Zhou is indeed a critical issue that urgently needs to be resolved. I will now write down my humble opinions as follows:

1. Shop clerks of the intellectual class: Can use their spare time to create more anti-Japanese and national salvation propaganda materials and send them to relevant national salvation organizations to serve as propaganda materials.

2. Shop clerks with relatively high incomes: Can save on all unnecessary expenses and donate to national salvation funds.

3. Regardless of whether you are a shop clerk, worker, or apprentice: You must secretly monitor at all times whether there is any "private entry of enemy goods" or "disguised domestic goods camouflaged to pass as enemy goods" in the store. Once discovered, you can anonymously report it to the relevant national salvation organizations so that a thorough investigation can be conducted; but you must strictly maintain secrecy to avoid the risk of losing your job.

Whether the above three points are appropriate, I hope readers will express their great opinions. Lu Fengzhao, December 5th

Editor:

We came to the store to work as an apprentice in order to solve the problem of earning a living. Naturally, we cannot help but be conscientious in our duties all day long. From this point of view, wouldn't it be that we have no spare time to take care of other things? "Can we allow the enemy who is killing our compatriots and invading our territory" to run rampant in our country? No, absolutely not! ··· Then should we take up spears and guns to drive him out? No··· Taking up spears and guns to drive him out is certainly the only way out; but if we act as an apprentice in this old-fashioned store, we are subject to all kinds of constraints and it will naturally be very difficult to do so.

However, within the scope of what is possible for us, there are "many ways" in which we can fulfill the obligations of a citizen of the Republic of China and engage in the work of resisting Japan and saving the nation. For example: everyday appliances: purchase domestic goods as much as possible. For food and clothing, do not purchase enemy goods; and even more so, do not sell enemy goods. Every time you have free time, going to amusement parks, smoking, drinking and other waste: you may wish to deduct a tenth of it each month to donate to the northeastern anti-Japanese heroes. If you encounter your friends, fellow villagers, relatives, or those who lack knowledge: you may wish to verbally publicize the various inhuman and vile acts of the Japanese pirates! So that all our compatriots will deeply imprint in their hearts the impression of a "foreign devil as our enemy"! All of these are easy to do, without any loss to individuals. Patriotic comrades will surely express their sympathy. If everyone in the business community can implement this, there is no way it will not be effective! At the same time, we "can fulfill the obligations of a citizen of the Republic of China and engage in the work of resisting Japan and saving the nation."

Respectfully submitted by Hu Mianong, December 5th

There is no need to talk loftily about resisting Japan; it is necessary to practically save the nation. However, to save the nation, one must first save the local area; to save the local area, one must first save one's own family; to save one's own family, one must first save oneself. Is one's own knowledge and ability worthy of such a major responsibility? If not, one must remedy one's own knowledge and ability. If one's own family is so economically oppressed that it cannot recover, do you feel the pain of your parents and wife? If not, you must first alleviate the oppression of your own family and ensure that your parents and wife have adequate needs in life. Take another look at the fact that there are many, many poor compatriots in your own village. How do you help them move towards a path of joy? In short: Don't set your ambitions too high or too far away. Choose what you can do within your ability and do your best. This is the true way to save the nation. If this is the case, then even if you do not resist Japan, you are already resisting it! Yao Kuangsheng's Answer

Novel

Writing to a Friend's Wife (Part 4 continued) 177

— Qin Shouou

Although the rain was pouring down like a waterfall, I didn't need to get wet at all because I had a rain hat, a raincoat, and a taxi readily available for business trips. I went from the office to the entrance of the alley in Ping An Li where you live. My heart was jumping like boiling water, and I got out of the car very slowly. At that time, the wall clock in the cigarette shop at the entrance of the alley was striking twelve. Noon on Sunday, September 10th.

Having decided to leave, why did I brave the rain to come here? Needless to say, the purpose was naturally to have one more meal at your house—to eat one last meal, to bid you a final farewell.

Speaking of "final farewell," I can't help but express some profound words that are enough to infuriate myself. To speak frankly: on the battlefield of a love triangle, when one of them suddenly expresses his intention to painfully give up love and head towards the object of his love to say Goodbye, it is less of a "final farewell" than a last-ditch effort, a do-or-die battle. He is by no means sincerely prepared to sacrifice, by no means passive; he is still struggling, still fighting. He just wants to change his method and use "death" or "running away" as a threat to snatch his loved one from the hands of his rival!

At that time, I didn't need to deny that that's exactly what I was thinking!

"Uncle Zhu······Eh······Uncle Zhu······Hahaha····!" But Zhou Dajing got the better of me. As soon as I jumped into the alley, I found a barrier stronger than a barbed wire mesh sandbag: what was that? That was your lovely "Little Rose." She was in Wu Ma's arms, holding a paper umbrella, aimlessly admiring the symphony of rain and human voices. She saw me as usual and opened her small mouth to laugh. At the same time, she stretched out two small arms as white as jade carvings and waved at me constantly. She was really as lovely as a little angel, and I frantically kissed her small cheeks in the heavy rain.

"Uncle····Uncle····Come·····Mama····Good!" These two short sentences of Zhu Chengwen that I was used to hearing were lightly uttered from her two lips, as bright as red roses; as soon as they met the air, they immediately transformed into the electric light emitted by an X-ray lamp, leaving me no room to escape and nakedly revealing the sinister thoughts I harbored.

"If the truth were as perfect as my fantasy—if you really jumped out of Dajing's house and followed me away—then wouldn't this "Little Rose" immediately become a "motherless child"? How sad would she be? How pitiful? ···" My thoughts suddenly took a turn, shifting towards moral considerations.

The arm with which I was holding Little Rose's little hand was shaking as if electrified. I don't know where the hot tears came from, but they jumped out of my eyes and dripped little by little on her golden, silky hair.

"Uncle Zhu···Uncle···Haha····Boy wants!" She meant that she wanted me to go in with her.

She won! The tense and sharp air was forcing me to retreat. I frantically threw away my rain hat, tore off my raincoat, and forgot everything as I rushed into the rain, where every drop was as big as a walnut. I don't know how much time passed or what places I went through, but I finally ended up decorated by the rain as a drenched drowned chicken, perched in a Russian restaurant on Avenue Joffre, drinking ice cream like crazy.

Speaking of drinking ice cream, I was reminded of the memorable old scene of this summer when you and I were fighting over ice cream at the Gaogiao seaside.

That day, I don't know what wind changed direction, but that level-headed, lethargic Zhu lawyer of yours suddenly had a whim and actually took the lead in enthusiastically proposing to go to the Gaogiao Seaside Bathing Beach; of course, I was the most enthusiastic supporter of this proposal. Unexpectedly, he then issued an order, assigning you to take care of Little Rose at home; as soon as he said this, I was as disappointed and uncomfortable as if I had been sentenced to life imprisonment. However, my beautiful piglet, am I not a famous character full of quick wit? A character full of quick wit will never be embarrassed. While I was disappointed, I was already planning a strategy for how to escape halfway—escaping halfway is my number one forte in life. Fortunately, there were two other characters nearby who were good at adding fun, and they had already withdrawn Dajing's order by means of rape and escorted you out the door.

Movie Special

Monday, December 12, 1932 (No extra charge)

Overseas News

Chaplin in London 178

— Yi Lie

Excerpt from *My Trip Abroad*

In 1931, when Chaplin returned to London from Hollywood, he received a total of more than 73,000 welcome letters in the first three days, averaging 1,111 letters per hour. To deal with the mountains of letters, Chaplin hired half a dozen temporary secretaries to open them.

Among these many letters, more than 28,000 were requests for charity. The amounts requested ranged from four dimes to four thousand dollars.

According to the explanations in these many letters, Chaplin had 680 parents in the UK. And they were all still alive, and the people who wrote to him said they were all cousins. Some even sent extremely detailed family trees as proof. Among the many charity requests, one was written like this:

"Mr. Chaplin! This letter contains the pawn ticket for my grandmother's gold tooth and silver teapot. You can see that the deadline for the pawn ticket has already expired yesterday. So please redeem it for me. As long as you pay the interest, you can renew the pawn date. Please, please! This way, my grandmother's mouth will have a day to welcome the gold tooth back. We have not been able to show our faces in front of our neighbors since my father pawned the silver pot to buy beer! From Little Friend"

Here are some of the most interesting letters:

"I, the undersigned, express my heartfelt welcome to Mr. Chaplin. I have arranged to come to shave Mr. Chaplin's beard on Sunday, September 11th, at your convenience. Sincerely, XX."

Another letter reads:

"Oh, admirable and enviable Mr. Chaplin, if you have any old leather shoes, please be kind enough to give me a pair, and I am willing to exchange them for a gold bracelet."

In Paris, a cinema asked him to sign the movie tickets, because all the signed tickets could be sold for one hundred francs each, and they were still "in short supply."

Movie Reviews

On *Breaking the Record* 179

— Star

After the many-big-star-studded *Radio Big Broadcast*, the screen at the Grand Theatre has been lively for several days. Since yesterday, it has changed to *Once in a Lifetime* (*Breaking the Record*). It is said to be another good work co-starred by many famous actors. So the front of the Grand Theatre is as lively as it has been for the past few days!

This story is adapted from a very famous script. It tells the story of a lucky guy who was originally an actor on the stage. Because the talkies were booming, he made an appointment with two colleagues and went to Hollywood. After some twists and turns, he unexpectedly succeeded. From then on, he rose to prominence, gaining both fame and fortune.

In terms of its plot, it would indeed be better to use the original name *Hollywood Happiness*. The Grand Theatre uses the empty *Breaking the Record* as the film title advertisement, which is of course easier to attract people, but it is too far from the main topic.

In films produced in capitalist countries, it is inevitable that there will be class colors. So American films, especially those with a comedic nature, will not be exceptions; this film takes this ready-made path. The god of fate turns a lucky guy who is completely incapable into a big shot, winning the laughter of the audience in an economic society. This is also a clear expression of the American tendency to always have a fluke mentality.

A Collection of Overseas Anecdotes 180

— Mei Cun

Howard Hughes, a wealthy Hollywood producer, is now planning to work for American Airlines. When he went to the company to apply, he changed his name to Charles W. Howard. He passed the exam completely, and the company has approved him for a pilot position. In the future, he also plans to use his experience in the sky to write a script and shoot an aviation film.

Thelma Todd's bed is the most spacious among Hollywood stars. It is about nine and a half feet wide and has two telephones on each side. She and her lover Pat de Ciccio each use one.

After completing her latest film, Roucho, Florentine Bros intends to go to China with her husband, John Gilbert, for their honeymoon.

In this so-called comedy, all the laughs are hidden in the dialogue and small actions. As a whole, it is just a comedy. However, director Russell Mack used his cleverness and worked very hard at satire, depicting the fickleness of the world and a kind of despicable behavior of wolves pretending to be tigers. I think; don't think it's funny, it's sad. In today's society, it can be seen everywhere, but we usually don't pay attention, and we can't see the specific facts!

The camera work is very clever. The lighting is also good. The transitions are very powerful. The overall organization and performance of the film are excellent. There are many small insertions, and the places where they are used are appropriate, adding a lot of interest.

Several actors perform a kind of intense emotion in a cold and witty way, sometimes making people feel indescribable—it's not simply laughable. Jack Oakie is certainly good. Even the other supporting roles are impeccable.

Reader Opinions

"Please Line Up" 181

— Chen Zhengfan

Not abiding by public order—this is a virtue of our noble people. Leaving aside everything else, just the scene in front of the ticket office of the movie theater, where people charge and crash, forming a tsunami of humanity, waving their fists and sleeves, and desperately rushing to be first, is enough to see! The backwardness of the national cultural level is so great that it makes people sigh!

"I" have never been abroad, so I dare not talk about the situation in foreign countries. During my summer vacation this year, I traveled north and lived in Tianjin for a month. In the evenings when the lights were on, I often went to the Grand Theater to watch movies. There, a wooden sign was hung high above the ticket office, with the words "Please Line Up" written on it. All the people buying tickets (both Chinese and foreigners) had to line up in a long snake formation according to the order of arrival, and buy tickets one by one in order. There was absolutely no mutual crowding or scrambling for the front. As a result, the staff members were refreshed and efficient. In just a short time, everyone was able to buy their tickets.

Owners of all large and small movie theaters in Shanghai, in order to make it easier for your own staff to do their jobs, and in order to cultivate the habit of abiding by public order among the people, may I ask you to implement this in the same way?

Celebrity Anecdotes

Ramon Novarro's Success Story (Part 1) 182

— Xi Meng

Fourteen years ago, Ramon Novarro was still a nineteen-year-old boy. He crossed the border from Durango, Mexico, into the United States to try his luck. When he went to the United States, in addition to youth and strength, he had incomplete English; he had no money and no friends. But he came to the United States regardless. At that time, the war between the United States and Mexico had ended not long ago, and the people of the two countries harbored resentment and hated each other. Therefore, Ramon Novarro's departure from Mexico to the United States was strongly opposed and worried about by his family. When Ramon arrived in the United States, from the snobbish perspective of the Americans, he was just an ordinary immigrant.

But Ramon is a very strange person. He is used to making a living in adversity and suffering. If you tell him that he cannot do something, he will listen to you, do it for you, and prove you wrong. He relies on this method and believes that he has divine assistance in resisting people. This courage of course helped him succeed.

At that time, the salaries of movie stars were not as high as they are now, but he once said: "If other actors can earn a thousand dollars a week, I can also earn a thousand dollars a week." At that time, he probably only earned a thousand copper coins a week, because he had just gotten some things to do.

After Ramon arrived in the United States, he joined Marie Mulligan's dance troupe, and when he had nothing to do, he was bound to find something to do. At that time, he did not have a definite goal, but he believed in himself and that he would definitely succeed in the future.

Domestic Film Preview

War Films and *The Lost Soldiers* 183

— Liao Zhai

During the scarlet fever epidemic of silent films, war films on the screen seemed to be dominated by *The Flower of the Battlefield*. When talkies suddenly rose, this glory seemed to be taken over by *All Quiet on the Western Front*. Scientific slaughter, in the electric light and shadows, still has the possibility of grabbing the minds of movie fans. Recently, the domestic film industry has also been infected with this terrifying and dangerous disease, but the facts prove that there is always a huge difference compared to imported goods. No wonder, this is due to the lack of materials, science, skills, and everything else. Perhaps an equal result can be achieved after a few years. Recently, in the domestic film industry, there are several well-known staff members who have jointly founded a film company, gathered various talents, and used extremely clever and great ideas to shoot a military film. The name of this film is called *The Lost Soldiers*.

The theme of *The Lost Soldiers* includes "loyalty, courage, filial piety, and righteousness." It takes the battlefield as the background, the secret work in the battlefield as the center, and then uses love to set off filial piety and righteousness. Chen Tian, the director of this play, himself is a cadre who once presided over secret work during the war. The real situation of the plot is a true depiction of his personal experience, more tragic than slaughter, and more dangerous than hand-to-hand combat, but you will not see any cruel images.

After the release of Lianhua's *Humanity*, moviegoers seemed to have a desire for appreciation. The birth of *The Lost Soldiers* may satisfy you even more. Now, it is said that the film is more than half completed. The military part is assisted by a certain army, which is actually more real than pretending.

We are eager for domestic films to produce better war films. We hope that *The Lost Soldiers* will have better results. We are looking forward to it here.

Casual Talk

Our Young Male Leads 184

— Tang Shen

In recent years, Chinese films are said to have been revived!

The martial arts genre of *Burning XX Temple* and *Breaking XXX* has finally disappeared from the market, and what has replaced them is the butterfly genre of films. Although some people are trying their best to advocate for the masses and for the nation, in fact, they are rarely seen, and even when they exist, they are forced.

The fact is that it is the turn of the butterfly genre; the position of the young male leads cannot but be important.

"Young male leads"—young male leads who make men envious and women intoxicated; you are also pioneers on the road to the revival of film. I hope that you will not indulge in wine and sex, but work hard to build the foundation of the Chinese film industry. With your hard work, there is no doubt that in the near future, you will make this silent world of young male leads shine brightly!

I think the following young male leads still have some status in the film industry; I have never met any of them, and I am only writing my piecemeal thoughts based on the impressions on the screen.

Jin Yan: He was previously in the Nanguo Drama Club, replacing Chen Ningqiu's position. He had already enjoyed great fame on the stage. The disadvantage at that time was a pair of strained eyes; but when he got to the screen, a pair of slightly open eyes (?), on the contrary, made the girls even more intoxicated. Recently, he has been promoted to the throne of emperor. He has a strong body, and his expressions can also be brought into full play. In fact, his fame is not due to this, but to the good director's script and good supporting actors that made him like this.

Zheng Junli: He was first discovered on the screen in *Wild Rose*. Later, after being discovered by Sun Yu, he was made the leading role in *Volcano Love Blood*, and recently he played the leading role in *Struggle*. Both have received good reviews.

Zhu Fei: His specialty is playing weak and sentimental men. His history on the screen is very long. Since Mingxing reopened, he has started to serve as the young male lead, with only a few retirements in between; he has no stable position. Since he went to jail in the north last year, he hasn't been heard from. I hope he will work hard to climb back onto the film stage in time.

Zheng Xiaoqiu: I have heard some old ladies say that he is good, but I can't think of what he is good at. Ying told me: "Isn't his fair and plump appearance and sincere and dull attitude the son that old ladies love in their hearts?" My feeling is that Zheng Xiaoqiu's handsomeness seems to have left the era.

Gong Jia Nong: The wrinkles on his forehead are not without a feeling of a beauty's fading years; however, his expression is very good. If there is a good script, and he plays a person around thirty years old, his achievements will be considerable. Those who have seen *Songstress Red Peony* and *Tearful Smile History* will definitely think that what I said is correct.

Sun Min: Some people say that this guy is a barber. Perhaps it is because when he puts on Western clothes, his head often stretches on top of him. I dare not compliment him on his handsomeness, but his body is just right. If he can put more research into his facial expressions and remove the colors of civilized drama from his actions, he can also be a very good young male lead.

Ma Lou Fen: A horse, though ugly, is fragrant everywhere. Isn't it strange? Mr. Ma, please don't be angry. Isn't your lullaby very popular? You should still give up the effort of painting and specialize in music.

Gao Zhanfei: His *Pink Dream*, *Southern Spring*, *Going to the National Crisis* and Jin Yan can almost stand side by side. What he is inferior to Jin Yan is that he cannot thoroughly understand the meaning of the plot, so sometimes the facial expressions do not work.

Chen Yitang: A twenty-one or two year old guy with a thin chin. I have only worshiped his film once, so I dare not determine. Then I don't know about Chen Qiufeng Wang Chunyuan.
